# Resrv v6 — Pre-Release Code Review Report

> Final review of the `v6-upgrade` branch (Statamic 5→6, Vue 2→3, Rates, parent/child cart flow, multiple payment gateways) before release.

## How this was produced

Twenty parallel review agents swept the entire codebase (188 PHP files, 45 Vue files, 15 Livewire components) — one per subsystem, plus dedicated cross-cutting **security**, **performance**, and **concurrency** sweeps. Every finding was then re-checked by an **independent verifier agent** that re-read the code, confirmed or refuted it, recalibrated severity, and ran targeted PHPUnit tests where applicable.

- **243** raw findings → **235** survived verification (185 confirmed, 50 partially-confirmed) → **208** after de-duplicating overlaps between the cross-cutting sweeps and the subsystem reviews.
- **7 refuted** and **1 uncertain** finding are listed in the appendix for transparency (do not action).
- Severity was recalibrated by the verifiers; there are **no `critical` findings** (all high-impact issues require an authenticated actor or a misconfiguration, not anonymous exploitation).

## How to use this report

Each item is a checkbox. Work top-down (High → Nit). When an item is fixed, change `- [ ]` to `- [x]`. Each item carries a stable ID (e.g. `H1`, `M12`) — reference it in commits/PRs. Items within a severity are grouped by subsystem area so related fixes batch together. Where a `Verify:` line names a test, run it after the fix; where it says *(no test)*, add one.

**Suggested order:** fix the High security/financial/correctness items first (`H`), then run the full suite (`composer test`), then proceed through Medium → Low → Nit.

## High-severity quick index

- **H1** — Webhook signature is forgeable when stripe_webhook_secret is empty (config default) — `src/Http/Payment/StripePaymentGateway.php`
- **H2** — $appends=['entry'] forces a Statamic stache lookup per row, plus lazy rate/childs/customer N+1 in list & calendar — `src/Models/Reservation.php`
- **H3** — ExpireReservations loads ALL pending reservations and runs synchronously on every availability search — `src/Jobs/ExpireReservations.php`
- **H4** — Parent/child reservation IDs collide in the shared availability `pending` array, causing missed decrements (overbooking) and wrong restores — `src/Listeners/DecreaseAvailability.php`
- **H5** — Deletion guard checks the localized entry id, not the origin id, so localizations delete despite active reservations — `src/Listeners/PreventEntryDeletionWithActiveReservations.php`
- **H6** — days_to_reservation condition uses now()->setHour(0) instead of startOfDay(), causing an off-by-one in days-until-reservation — `src/Models/DynamicPricing.php`
- **H7** — Price::create hardcodes *100, breaking all non-2-decimal currencies (JPY, BHD, KWD, etc.) — `src/Money/Price.php`
- **H8** — Time-window condition is broken for same-day windows and misses early hours of overnight windows — `src/Models/ExtraCondition.php`
- **H9** — CP routes do not enforce the 'use resrv' permission — any CP user can refund payments, edit availability, delete data — `routes/cp.php`
- **H10** — Reservation search queries a dropped `customer` column — search is completely broken (500) — `src/Http/Controllers/ReservationCpController.php`
- **H11** — N+1 queries in the CP reservations listing (customer, extras, options, rate, childs.rate, entry per row) — `src/Http/Controllers/ReservationCpController.php`
- **H12** — Extra quantity has no server-side min/max validation, allowing negative quantities that reduce the amount charged — `src/Livewire/Forms/EnabledExtras.php`
- **H13** — Stored XSS: affiliate name rendered with v-html — `resources/js/components/AffiliatesList.vue`
- **H14** — Entry link in reservations listing never renders (wrong/missing property) — `resources/js/pages/Reservations/Index.vue`

---

## 🔴 High (14)

### Payments & Webhooks

- [x] **H1 — Webhook signature is forgeable when stripe_webhook_secret is empty (config default)**
  - **Where:** `src/Http/Payment/StripePaymentGateway.php:123-134, 247`
  - **Problem:** getWebhookSecret() returns config('resrv-config.stripe_webhook_secret'), whose default in config/config.php:122 is '' (env RESRV_STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET default ''). For the multisite array form it returns null when the reservation's collection handle is absent from the array. That value is passed straight to Webhook::constructEvent → WebhookSignature::computeSignature, which does hash_hmac('sha256', $payload, $secret). With an empty/null secret the HMAC key is empty and publicly known, so an attacker can compute a valid v1= signature and forge the Stripe-Signature header, fully defeating verification on a CSRF-exempt endpoint. A site that deploys Stripe without configuring the webhook secret (or a multisite collection missing from the array) accepts forged webhooks — enabling the cancel path on PENDING reservations and spamming the orphan-payment path. The code never rejects an empty/null secret.
  - **Fix:** In verifyPayment, before constructEvent: `$secret = $this->getWebhookSecret($reservation); if (! is_string($secret) || $secret === '') { Log::error('Stripe webhook secret not configured'); abort(500); }`. Optionally fail fast at boot when Stripe is the gateway but no webhook secret is set.
  - **Evidence:** config/config.php:122 `'stripe_webhook_secret' => env('RESRV_STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET', '')`. Gateway getWebhookSecret() (123-134) returns the bare config value or null when the handle is missing from the array, with no empty check. WebhookSignature.php:138 `return hash_hmac('sha256', $payload, $secret)` — empty/known secret means a forgeable HMAC. Route web.php:10 is `withoutMiddleware([VerifyCsrfToken::class])`, so the only auth is the signature.
  - _security · confirmed · high confidence_

### Reservations & State machine

- [x] **H2 — $appends=['entry'] forces a Statamic stache lookup per row, plus lazy rate/childs/customer N+1 in list & calendar**
  - **Where:** `src/Models/Reservation.php:46,143-148`
  - **Problem:** protected $appends = ['entry'] makes getEntryAttribute() (line 143) run on every array/JSON serialization, doing Entry::find($this->item_id) — a Statamic stache lookup — per row. ReservationResource::toArray() additionally reads $reservation->customer (BelongsTo relation; the 'customer' column was dropped in migration 2025_03_20_000005 and replaced by a customer_id FK + customer() relation, so this IS a lazy relation load, not a column), ->extras, ->options, and getRateLabel() (which lazy-loads ->rate and, for parents, ->childs). ReservationCpController::getReservations() applies only orderBy/where and NO ->with(), so each paginated row triggers a stache lookup plus several relation queries. ReservationCalendarResource has the same shape (line 74 reads $reservation->entry['title'], plus getRateLabel()/->childs) and calendar() (lines 67-71) eager-loads nothing. For a page of N reservations this is N stache lookups + N*(customer, extras, options, rate) queries. show() is fine — it explicitly eager-loads (line 95). Severity high is justified for a busy CP list/calendar.
  - **Fix:** Eager-load relations in getReservations()/calendar() (e.g. ->with(['rate','customer','extras','options','childs.rate'])). For entries, batch-resolve by item_id once per page or drop 'entry' from $appends and resolve only where needed (show() already resolves it explicitly).
  - **Evidence:** Line 46 `protected $appends = ['entry']`. Lines 143-148 getEntryAttribute() does Entry::find($this->item_id). ReservationResource lines 47,53,54,55,56 read entry/customer/extras/options/getRateLabel per row. getReservations() (controller 236-248) only does orderBy/where — no with(). calendar() (controller 67-71) only orderBy. Migration 2025_03_20_000005 drops the 'customer' column; customer() is a BelongsTo (Reservation.php:58).
  - _performance · confirmed · high confidence · also independently flagged by: xc-performance, xc-concurrency sweep(s)_

### Lifecycle (events / listeners / jobs)

- [x] **H3 — ExpireReservations loads ALL pending reservations and runs synchronously on every availability search**
  - **Where:** `src/Jobs/ExpireReservations.php:29-39`
  - **Problem:** handle() loads the ENTIRE pending set with Reservation::where('status', PENDING)->get() then computes expiry in PHP per row (created_at + minutes_to_hold). dispatchSync() is called on every availability search (Availability::getAvailable line 72, getAvailabilityForEntry line 82). So every search loads all PENDING rows and filters in PHP. The SQL-filter and early-return improvements are valid and worthwhile. Two corrections to the finding: (1) the minutes_to_hold==false early-return is ALREADY above the ->get() (lines 30-32 return before line 33), so 'it re-runs even when minutes_to_hold would have excluded everything' is wrong — only the session-based single expire at line 27-29 runs in that case, which is a single find() by id. (2) Severity: real and on a hot path, but PENDING is a small, self-pruning subset (only un-converted holds within the hold window plus stragglers), not a full-table scan, so medium-to-high rather than clearly high. The expensive part is the unconditional per-search prune pass, not the row count.
  - **Fix:** Filter stale rows in SQL: Reservation::where('status', PENDING)->where('created_at', '<=', now()->subMinutes($holdMinutes))->get() so only actually-expired rows are loaded and the PHP loop disappears. Additionally consider throttling the sync dispatch (e.g. cache a 'last pruned at' timestamp and prune at most every N seconds, or move to a scheduled queue worker) so not every single search triggers a prune pass. The minutes_to_hold early-return is already correctly placed.
  - **Evidence:** Lines 30-33: `if (config('resrv-config.minutes_to_hold', false) == false) { return; } $pending = Reservation::where('status', ReservationStatus::PENDING->value)->get();` — early-return IS present before the ->get(). Lines 34-39 loop in PHP computing Carbon::parse(created_at)->add(minutes) per row. Availability.php line 72 `ExpireReservations::dispatchSync();` in getAvailable, line 82 in getAvailabilityForEntry.
  - _performance · partially-confirmed · high confidence · also independently flagged by: reservation-lifecycle, xc-concurrency, availability-core sweep(s)_

- [x] **H4 — Parent/child reservation IDs collide in the shared availability `pending` array, causing missed decrements (overbooking) and wrong restores**
  - **Where:** `src/Listeners/DecreaseAvailability.php:28-42`
  - **Problem:** The `resrv_availabilities.pending` column is a JSON array (migration 2024_06_29_093843, cast 'array' in Models/Availability.php:45) that stores bare integer reservation IDs. Normal reservations store their `resrv_reservations` PK (DecreaseAvailability::handle -> decrementAvailability -> reservationId: $event->reservation->id), while a parent's children store their `resrv_child_reservations` PK (decreaseMultiple -> reservationId: $child->id). These are two independent auto-increment sequences both starting at 1. addToPending() (AvailabilityRepository.php:249-265) guards with `in_array($reservationId, $pending)` on the bare integer and removeFromPending() (267-283) uses `array_diff($pending, [$reservationId])` — neither can distinguish a child id from a normal id. When a normal reservation and a child reservation that happen to share the same integer id both target the SAME availability row, the second decrement is silently skipped (logged + `continue`) => overbooking; on release, removing the shared integer restores stock belonging to the other holder. Note the same row can be hit even WITHOUT shared rates: a normal reservation booking rate X and a parent-cart child booking rate X over overlapping dates both lock and write the identical resrv_availabilities rows. The `isChildReservation` flag exists but is only passed to validateMaxAvailableForDateRange — it is NOT propagated into addToPending/removeFromPending, so the pending array truly cannot namespace the two id-spaces.
  - **Fix:** Namespace the pending entries by reservation type so the two id-spaces cannot collide. E.g. in decreaseMultiple/incrementMultiple pass a prefixed key ('c'.$child->id) and in handle() ('r'.$reservation->id), and update addToPending/removeFromPending (and the in_array/array_diff checks) to operate on those string keys; or store structured entries like ['type'=>'child','id'=>...]. Thread isChildReservation all the way down to addToPending/removeFromPending so the key can be derived consistently. Add a regression test that creates a normal reservation and a parent+child reservation with matching integer ids against one shared/identical availability row and asserts both holds are subtracted.
  - **Evidence:** Migration: `$table->json('pending')->nullable();`. Cast: `'pending' => 'array'`. addToPending: `if (in_array($reservationId, $pending)) { Log::error(...); continue; } ... 'pending' => array_merge($pending, [$reservationId])`. removeFromPending: `array_values(array_diff($pending, [$reservationId]))`. decreaseMultiple passes `reservationId: $child->id`; handle passes `reservationId: $event->reservation->id`. ChildReservation uses table `resrv_child_reservations` — a separate sequence from `resrv_reservations`.
  - _bug · confirmed · high confidence_

- [x] **H5 — Deletion guard checks the localized entry id, not the origin id, so localizations delete despite active reservations**
  - **Where:** `src/Listeners/PreventEntryDeletionWithActiveReservations.php:18`
  - **Problem:** PreventEntryDeletionWithActiveReservations::handle() calls ActiveReservationsGuard::hasActiveReservationsForEntry($event->entry->id()) using the raw id off the event. Reservations are always stored with the ORIGIN id (HandlesReservationQueries.php:82/131 sets 'item_id' => $this->entryId, and AvailabilityResults.php:70 sets $this->entryId = $this->getDefaultSiteEntry($entry)->id(), which resolves to origin()). Statamic's multisite 'Delete' action (vendor DeleteMultisiteEntry::run, behavior !== copy) calls $items->each->deleteDescendants(), which deletes every localization FIRST (Entry::deleteDescendants -> each $entry->delete()), and Entry::delete() dispatches EntryDeleting BEFORE the 'cannot delete with localizations' check. For a localization, $event->entry->id() !== the origin id, so the guard's WHERE item_id = <localized id> matches no reservation and returns false; the localization is hard-deleted. Only the subsequent origin delete is blocked. Net result: deleting a booked item in multisite wipes its localizations while leaving the origin + reservations intact - an inconsistent state where bookings reference an item whose translations vanished. The single-site path is correctly tested (PreventEntryDeletionWithActiveReservationsTest, 4 passing) but there is NO multisite deletion test covering this gap.
  - **Fix:** Resolve to origin before the guard check: $id = $event->entry->hasOrigin() ? $event->entry->origin()->id() : $event->entry->id(); then pass $id to hasActiveReservationsForEntry (and to the log payload). The Statamic Entry passed on the event exposes hasOrigin()/origin(). This blocks deletion of any localization of a booked item.
  - **Evidence:** Guard: `if (ActiveReservationsGuard::hasActiveReservationsForEntry($event->entry->id()))` (line 18). Guard query: `Reservation::where('item_id', $statamicId)->whereNotIn('status', ReservationStatus::terminal())->exists()` (ActiveReservationsGuard.php:16-18). Reservation stores origin id: `'item_id' => $this->entryId` (HandlesReservationQueries.php:82) where `$this->entryId = $this->getDefaultSiteEntry($entry)->id()` (AvailabilityResults.php:70). Delete order: `$items->each->deleteDescendants()` (DeleteMultisiteEntry.php:56), `deleteDescendants` -> `$entry->delete()` per descendant (Entry.php:293-295), and `delete()` fires `EntryDeleting::dispatch($this)` at line 258 before the descendants guard at line 262. MultisiteAvailabilityTest asserts data is keyed by origin id (availability_is_stored_with_origin_entry_id, lines 166-177).
  - _bug · confirmed · high confidence_

### Pricing & Money

- [x] **H6 — days_to_reservation condition uses now()->setHour(0) instead of startOfDay(), causing an off-by-one in days-until-reservation**
  - **Where:** `src/Models/DynamicPricing.php:446-450`
  - **Problem:** checkCondition() computes `(int) Carbon::parse($date_start)->diffInDays(now()->setHour(0), true)` for the days_to_reservation branch. setHour(0) only zeroes the hour, leaving minutes/seconds, so at 15:30:45 the comparison anchor becomes 'today 00:30:45'. The leftover fractional day is truncated by (int), yielding one day fewer than reality. A reservation 3 calendar days out evaluates to 2, so last-minute rules like `days_to_reservation <= 2` fire a day early (and early-bird rules a day late). The sibling helper HandlesAvailabilityDates.php:48 computes the identical days-until-start using startOfDay(), confirming the inconsistency. No apply-level test covers days_to_reservation (DynamicPricingApplyTest covers reservation_duration, reservation_price, and date conditions only), so it is uncaught.
  - **Fix:** Use `now()->startOfDay()` (matching HandlesAvailabilityDates.php:48 and :102) and parse date_start via startOfDay for symmetry: `(int) Carbon::parse($date_start)->startOfDay()->diffInDays(now()->startOfDay(), true)`.
  - **Evidence:** Line 447: `... diffInDays(now()->setHour(0), true) ...`. Reproduced with Carbon::setTestNow('2026-05-29 15:30:45') and date_start 2026-06-01: setHour(0) anchor = '2026-05-29 00:30:45' -> 2 days; startOfDay() -> 3 days. HandlesAvailabilityDates.php:48 uses `Carbon::now()->startOfDay()` for the same concept. Test grep shows no days_to_reservation apply test.
  - _bug · confirmed · high confidence_

- [x] **H7 — Price::create hardcodes *100, breaking all non-2-decimal currencies (JPY, BHD, KWD, etc.)**
  - **Where:** `src/Money/Price.php:20-26`
  - **Problem:** create() builds Money via `new Money(bcmul($price, 100), new Currency(config('resrv-config.currency_isoCode')))`, always assuming 2-decimal subunits, while format() uses DecimalMoneyFormatter+ISOCurrencies which respects each currency's real subunit count. For a 0-decimal currency (JPY) 1000 round-trips to 100000 (100x too large); for a 3-decimal currency (BHD) 100 round-trips to 10.000 (10x too small). config/config.php (line 54) explicitly invites any ISO_4217 code, so any non-2-decimal currency is fully broken across storage, comparisons, and payment amounts.
  - **Fix:** Scale by the currency's actual subunit instead of the literal 100, or parse the decimal input with Money\Parser\DecimalMoneyParser (the inverse of the DecimalMoneyFormatter already used in format()), guaranteeing create()/format() symmetry for every currency.
  - **Evidence:** Line 23: `$class->money = new Money(bcmul($price, 100), new Currency(config('resrv-config.currency_isoCode')));` vs format() lines 101-104 using ISOCurrencies. I reproduced the round-trips: JPY 1000 -> 100000, BHD 100 -> 10.000, EUR 100 -> 100.00. The hardcoded 100 contradicts the currency-aware formatter.
  - _bug · confirmed · high confidence · also independently flagged by: availability-core sweep(s)_

### Extras / Options / Cutoff

- [x] **H8 — Time-window condition is broken for same-day windows and misses early hours of overnight windows**
  - **Where:** `src/Models/ExtraCondition.php:255-262`
  - **Problem:** checkTime() unconditionally does $time_end = Carbon::createFromTimeString($condition->time_end)->addDay(), then pins the payload to today() and checks between($time_start, $time_end). For a same-day window 09:00->17:00 the end becomes tomorrow 17:00, so the effective span is ~32h and a pickup at 20:00 is matched as in-range. For the intended overnight case 21:00->08:00 a pickup at 07:00 (which IS inside the overnight window) is NOT matched because the payload pinned to today 07:00 is below today 21:00. I reproduced both: checkTime('09:00','17:00','...20:00') => true (should be false); checkTime('21:00','08:00','...07:00') => false (should be true). This feeds both shouldApplyCondition() (required/hidden display logic) and checkAllParameters() (server-side required-extras enforcement), so it can wrongly require/hide extras and wrongly block or permit checkout.
  - **Fix:** Detect midnight wrap and map the payload onto the correct day, or compare minutes-of-day: start=h*60+m of time_start, end of time_end, t of pickup time, then result = wraps ? (t>=start || t<=end) : (t>=start && t<=end), where wraps = end<start. Add same-day and overnight (incl. early-morning) tests; none currently exist.
  - **Evidence:** ExtraCondition.php:257-261 $time_start=createFromTimeString(time_start); $time_end=createFromTimeString(time_end)->addDay(); $payload->setDateFrom(today())->between($time_start,$time_end). PHP repro against vendor Carbon confirmed the two wrong returns above. No test under tests/ exercises checkTime.
  - _correctness · confirmed · high confidence_

### CP / HTTP & Routing

- [x] **H9 — CP routes do not enforce the 'use resrv' permission — any CP user can refund payments, edit availability, delete data**
  - **Where:** `routes/cp.php:3-90`
  - **Problem:** The entire Resrv CP route group is registered via AddonServiceProvider::registerCpRoutes -> Statamic::pushCpRoutes, which the core injects inside the single `statamic.cp.authenticated` middleware group (vendor/statamic/cms/routes/cp.php:157 -> Statamic::additionalCpRoutes()). That group (defined in CpServiceProvider.php:93) contains only \Statamic\Http\Middleware\CP\Authorize, which checks `$user->cant('access cp')` and nothing else. The addon's `use resrv` permission is registered (ResrvProvider::bootPermissions) but is only applied to (a) the nav links via `->can('use resrv')` and (b) the three Export routes via `Route::middleware('can:use resrv')` (routes/cp.php:73-77). Every other endpoint — including reservation.refund (real gateway refund), availability.update/delete/clearStuckPending, rate/extra/option/affiliate/dataimport mutations, and utility.entries — has no `use resrv` gate, and no FormRequest enforces it (AffiliateCpRequest::authorize() returns true; the other requests omit authorize()). So any user with `access cp` can hit these. Severity recalibrated to high (not critical): exploitation still requires an authenticated CP account with `access cp`, i.e. a trusted-but-lower-privilege user, not an anonymous attacker; impact (real refunds, data deletion, overbooking via clearStuckPending) is severe within that population.
  - **Fix:** Wrap the outer route group in `Route::middleware('can:use resrv')` (apply to the whole `Route::namespace(...)->name('resrv.')` group) and drop the now-redundant inner Export middleware. Add a feature test that signs in a non-super user lacking `use resrv` and asserts 403 on reservation.refund and availability.update.
  - **Evidence:** vendor/statamic/cms/src/Providers/CpServiceProvider.php:93 `$router->middlewareGroup('statamic.cp.authenticated', [...]` includes only `\Statamic\Http\Middleware\CP\Authorize::class`. Authorize.php: `if ($user->cant('access cp')) { throw new AuthorizationException(...) }` — no `use resrv` check. routes/cp.php:73-77 is the ONLY `Route::middleware('can:use resrv')`; refund (line 57), availability.* (6-9), utility.entries (83), affiliate/extra/option/rate/dataimport routes have none. AffiliateCpRequest.php:16-19 `authorize() { return true; }`.
  - _security · confirmed · high confidence · also independently flagged by: reservation-core, affiliate-customer-data, xc-security sweep(s)_

- [x] **H10 — Reservation search queries a dropped `customer` column — search is completely broken (500)**
  - **Where:** `src/Http/Controllers/ReservationCpController.php:250-264`
  - **Problem:** searchReservations() builds `->where('customer', 'like', $searchTerm)` (line 256). The `customer` json column that existed since 2021_05_04_160454_create_reservations_table.php was dropped by 2025_03_20_000005_drop_customer_column_from_reservations_table.php. The model no longer has a `customer` column or `getCustomerAttribute` accessor — `customer()` is now a BelongsTo to Customer (Reservation.php:58-61). Any search input routes getReservations() (line 243 `request()->filled('search')`) to searchReservations(), emitting `where "customer" like ?` against a non-existent column -> QueryException (500) on both SQLite and Postgres. CP reservation search is entirely broken. I confirmed the column is dropped and that index without search still works (test_can_index_reservations passes), so the break is isolated to the search path.
  - **Fix:** Replace the `customer` clause with a relation search, e.g. `->orWhereHas('customer', fn ($q) => $q->where('email', 'like', $searchTerm)->orWhere('name', 'like', $searchTerm))`, and add a feature test hitting `resrv.reservation.index?search=foo` asserting 200.
  - **Evidence:** ReservationCpController.php:256 `$query->where('customer', 'like', $searchTerm)`. Migration drop_customer_column: `$table->dropColumn('customer');`. Reservation.php:58 `public function customer(): BelongsTo { return $this->belongsTo(Customer::class, 'customer_id'); }` — no scalar `customer` column. No `getCustomerAttribute` in the model (grep of Reservation.php).
  - _bug · confirmed · high confidence_

- [x] **H11 — N+1 queries in the CP reservations listing (customer, extras, options, rate, childs.rate, entry per row)**
  - **Where:** `src/Http/Controllers/ReservationCpController.php:76-90, 236-248`
  - **Problem:** index() builds the query via getReservations() (lines 236-248) which only applies orderBy + optional search and adds NO eager loading, then paginates and hands the page to ReservationResource. ReservationResource::toArray (lines 41-62) accesses per row: $reservation->entry (appended -> getEntryAttribute, a Statamic Entry::find + toAugmentedArray), $reservation->customer (lazy BelongsTo), $reservation->extras and ->options (lazy BelongsToMany, both withTrashed), and $reservation->getRateLabel() which lazy-loads $this->rate (Reservation.php:135) or for parents lazy-loads $this->childs and each child's ->rate (Reservation.php:128-133). So a page of N rows fires on the order of N*(4-6) DB queries plus N Statamic stache lookups. show() (line 95) correctly eager-loads, proving index() is the outlier.
  - **Fix:** Eager load on the index query before paginate(): $this->reservation->with(['customer', 'extras', 'options', 'rate', 'childs.rate']). The entry/stache lookup needs separate handling (see the $appends finding) — resolve entries in a single batch per page or drop them from the appended attribute.
  - **Evidence:** ReservationCpController::index lines 78-83: $query = $this->getReservations(); ... $query->paginate($perPage). getReservations lines 236-248 only does orderBy/search, no with(). ReservationResource lines 47/53/54/55/56 access entry/customer/extras/options/getRateLabel per row. show() line 95 uses ->with(['extras','options.values','affiliate','dynamicPricings','childs.rate']).
  - _performance · confirmed · high confidence · also independently flagged by: xc-performance sweep(s)_

### Frontend Livewire

- [x] **H12 — Extra quantity has no server-side min/max validation, allowing negative quantities that reduce the amount charged**
  - **Where:** `src/Livewire/Forms/EnabledExtras.php:40-43`
  - **Problem:** The only server-side gate on extra quantity is EnabledExtras::rules() which declares 'extras.*.quantity' => ['required','integer'] — no min/gt/max. The bounds check the reviewer cites lives only in the UI action Extras::updateExtraQuantity() (Extras.php:163: `if ($quantity > 0 && ($originalExtra->maximum == 0 || $quantity <= $originalExtra->maximum))`), which a client bypasses by dispatching the 'extras-updated' Livewire event directly. Checkout::updateExtras() (Checkout.php:546-550) assigns the raw payload to $this->enabledExtras->extras. The drift defence does NOT catch a negative/oversized quantity: in validateTotal() (Reservation.php:368/397-398) the DB side computes `Extra::find($id)->calculatePrice($data, $extra['quantity'])` using the SAME client quantity that calculateExtraTotals() (HandlesPricing.php:50) used for the frontend total, so both sides are equally negative and `$dbTotal->equals($frontendTotal)` passes (Reservation.php:371). Extra::calculatePrice → price->multiply($quantity) with no clamp (Extra.php:195-210, applyQuantityIfNeeded has no lower bound), and moneyphp permits negative amounts. handleFirstStep then writes the reduced figure into `total` and (when payment=='everything') `payment` (Checkout.php:194-205). Net effect: a crafted negative-quantity extra undercharges the booking. Severity high (financial), but real-world reach requires a valid extra id and direct event dispatch, hence medium confidence.
  - **Fix:** Add bounds to the rule: 'extras.*.quantity' => ['required','integer','min:1'], and enforce the per-extra maximum server-side against the authoritative Extra model in handleFirstStep/validateReservation (reject when maximum>0 && quantity>maximum). Do not rely on the UI-only check in updateExtraQuantity().
  - **Evidence:** EnabledExtras.php:40-43 rule is integer-only. extrasToSync() (line 16) calls $this->validate() but that enforces only the integer rule. Extras.php:163 enforces bounds but is reachable only via the updateExtraQuantity action, not the 'extras-updated' event handled at Checkout.php:546-550. validateTotal uses the same client quantity on both sides (Reservation.php:368, 397-398; HandlesPricing.php:50), so equals() passes for negatives. No clamp in Extra::calculatePrice/applyQuantityIfNeeded (Extra.php:159-211).
  - _security · confirmed · medium confidence · also independently flagged by: extras-options sweep(s)_

### Vue / CP UI

- [x] **H13 — Stored XSS: affiliate name rendered with v-html**
  - **Where:** `resources/js/components/AffiliatesList.vue:16`
  - **Problem:** AffiliatesList.vue line 16 renders the affiliate name as raw HTML: `<span ... v-html="item.name" @click="editAffiliate(item)"></span>`. The name is free-text entered in AffiliatesPanel.vue via `<Input v-model="form.name" />` (line 16) and stored/returned by AffiliateCpController without any HTML escaping (allAffiliates() returns the Eloquent collection as-is; AffiliateCpRequest does not strip HTML). A CP user who can create/edit affiliates can store a payload like `<img src=x onerror=alert(document.cookie)>` in the name, which then executes in the browser of any admin who opens the Affiliates list. The name is plain text and never needs v-html.
  - **Fix:** Replace `v-html="item.name"` with text interpolation: `<span ... @click="editAffiliate(item)">{{ item.name }}</span>`. No sanitizer or rich formatting is needed.
  - **Evidence:** Line 16: `<span class="... hover:underline" v-html="item.name" @click="editAffiliate(item)"></span>` renders raw HTML. The name source is AffiliatesPanel.vue line 16 `<Input v-model="form.name" />` and AffiliateCpController::allAffiliates() (lines 37-46) returns the model without escaping. Vue's default `{{ }}` would auto-escape; v-html deliberately bypasses that. This is a genuine stored XSS sink in CP-privileged code.
  - _security · confirmed · high confidence_

- [x] **H14 — Entry link in reservations listing never renders (wrong/missing property)**
  - **Where:** `resources/js/pages/Reservations/Index.vue:94-98`
  - **Problem:** The cell-entry slot only links the title when reservation.entry?.permalink is truthy, but the listing payload never carries a permalink key for real entries. ReservationResource (src/Resources/ReservationResource.php:47) sets 'entry' => $reservation->entry, and Reservation::getEntryAttribute() (src/Models/Reservation.php:143-148) returns Entry::find()->toAugmentedArray(['id', 'title', 'slug', 'url']). I verified in vendor that toAugmentedArray($keys) -> toAugmentedCollectionWithFields -> ->select($keys) (vendor/statamic/cms/src/Data/HasAugmentedInstance.php:33 and the toAugmentedCollectionWithFields method), so the resulting array contains ONLY id/title/slug/url - permalink is excluded even though Entry exposes a 'permalink' augmented key (Entry.php:1050,1127). Net effect is inverted: for every existing entry reservation.entry.permalink is undefined and the v-if is false, so the title renders as plain text (line 98); only a deleted entry, whose emptyEntry() fallback (src/Models/Reservation.php:615-623) returns 'permalink' => '#', would render an anchor - and it would point at '#'. The 'open entry in new tab' affordance is dead for all real reservations. No existing test catches this: test_can_index_reservations only assertSee($item->title).
  - **Fix:** Use the key that actually exists: <a v-if="reservation.entry?.url" :href="reservation.entry.url" target="_blank">. The url key is in the selected augmented keys and serializes to the entry URL string. Optionally drop 'permalink' => '#' from emptyEntry() (or add 'url' => null there) so deleted entries fall through to the plain-text <span v-else> branch and the data shape is consistent across real and deleted entries.
  - **Evidence:** Template (Index.vue:95): `<a v-if="reservation.entry?.permalink" :href="reservation.entry.permalink" target="_blank">`. Model (Reservation.php:147): `return $entry ? $entry->toAugmentedArray(['id', 'title', 'slug', 'url']) : $this->emptyEntry();` - no 'permalink' key. emptyEntry() (Reservation.php:621): `'permalink' => '#',`. Statamic select() filters keys, confirmed via HasAugmentedInstance::toAugmentedCollectionWithFields using ->select($keys).
  - _bug · confirmed · high confidence_

---

## 🟠 Medium (38)

### Payments & Webhooks

- [x] **M1 — Stripe webhook timestamp tolerance disabled — replay attacks possible**
  - **Where:** `src/Http/Payment/StripePaymentGateway.php:244-250`
  - **Problem:** verifyPayment() calls Webhook::constructEvent($payload, $sig_header, $secret, null, false). The vendor signature Webhook::constructEvent($payload,$sigHeader,$secret,$tolerance=self::DEFAULT_TOLERANCE) accepts only 4 params, so the 5th argument (false) is silently ignored and the 4th (null) overrides the default 300s tolerance. In WebhookSignature::verifyHeader the replay guard is `if (($tolerance > 0) && (abs(time()-$timestamp) > $tolerance))`; with null, `null > 0` is false so the timestamp check is skipped entirely. Stripe's replay defense is therefore disabled. Impact is real but bounded: a replayed signed payment_intent.succeeded is mitigated by the CONFIRMED short-circuit and transitionTo() no-op gating, and replayed canceled/payment_failed only act while the reservation is still PENDING; still, the primary replay protection is gone and the malformed call shape indicates author error.
  - **Fix:** Call Webhook::constructEvent($request->getContent(), $sig_header, $secret) (relying on DEFAULT_TOLERANCE=300) or pass an explicit Webhook::DEFAULT_TOLERANCE. Remove the stray 5th argument.
  - **Evidence:** Gateway line 244-250: `Webhook::constructEvent($request->getContent(), $sig_header, $this->getWebhookSecret($reservation), null, false)`. Vendor Webhook.php:27 signature is `constructEvent($payload, $sigHeader, $secret, $tolerance = self::DEFAULT_TOLERANCE)` (4 params; DEFAULT_TOLERANCE=300). WebhookSignature.php:66 `if (($tolerance > 0) && ...)` — with $tolerance=null this is false, skipping the timestamp check.
  - _security · confirmed · high confidence · also independently flagged by: xc-security sweep(s)_

### Reservations & State machine

- [x] **M2 — Price accessors invoke bcmul(null,...) when total (nullable, no default) is unset**
  - **Where:** `src/Models/Reservation.php:93-96,201-204`
  - **Problem:** The total column is float nullable with NO default (migration 2024_03_20_212538: `$table->float('total', 8, 2)->nullable()`). createReservation() and createMultiReservation() (HandlesReservationQueries.php:77-92 and 127-139) never set 'total' — it stays NULL until Checkout::*->update(['total' => ...]) (Checkout.php:617). Reading $reservation->total before that calls getTotalAttribute(null) -> Price::create(null) -> bcmul(null, 100). I verified on PHP 8.5 this emits 'Deprecated: bcmul(): Passing null to parameter #1 ($num1) of type string is deprecated' and returns '0'; under PHP 9 passing null to a string param becomes a TypeError. Because bcmul(null,100) returns 0, amountRemaining() (line 203, total->subtract(payment)) on a not-yet-checked-out reservation computes 0 - payment = a NEGATIVE remaining amount. The invariant that protects this is fragile (amountRemaining only used in made/confirmed emails fired after checkout sets total). Same null path applies to any nullable Price column read before assignment.
  - **Fix:** Make Price::create null-safe and PHP-9-ready: new Money(bcmul((string) ($price ?? 0), 100), ...). Optionally give total a ->default(0) in a migration + backfill, or guard accessors with Price::create($value ?? 0).
  - **Evidence:** Migration 2024_03_20_212538 line 17: float('total',8,2)->nullable() (no default). createReservation (HandlesReservationQueries 77-92) and createMultiReservation (127-139) omit 'total'. Checkout.php:617 sets it only at checkout. Price::create (Price.php:23) does bcmul($price, 100). Verified locally: `php -d error_reporting=E_ALL -r 'echo bcmul(null,100);'` => 'Deprecated: bcmul(): Passing null...' then '0'.
  - _correctness · confirmed · high confidence_
  - **Resolution:** The underlying mechanism was already eliminated by the **H7** fix, which replaced the `bcmul($price, 100)` body of `Price::create()` with a `DecimalMoneyParser` that maps the empty string from `(string) null` to `Money(0)` (Price.php:29-37; DecimalMoneyParser::parse() returns `new Money(0, …)` for `''`). Independently re-verified on PHP 8.5.6 with `--display-deprecations --display-warnings --display-notices`: `Price::create(null)` returns a zero Price with **no** deprecation/warning/TypeError. The `amountRemaining()` "negative remaining" path is only reachable from the made/confirmed emails, which fire after checkout sets `total`. ⚠️ The proposed fix must **NOT** be applied — reintroducing `bcmul(…, 100)` would regress H7 and re-break non-2-decimal currencies (JPY/BHD/KWD). Instead the null-safety contract is now locked by regression tests: `PriceTest::test_price_create_handles_null_as_zero` and `ReservationCheckoutTest::test_reading_total_before_checkout_returns_zero_price_without_error`.

### Availability & Rates

- [x] **M3 — Extra-days search repeats identical Rate and Entry queries once per generated period**
  - **Where:** `src/Livewire/Traits/HandlesAvailabilityQueries.php:79-99`
  - **Problem:** queryExtraAvailabilityForEntry() maps over generateDatePeriods() (2*extraDays+1 periods) and calls Availability::getAvailabilityForEntry() per period. Each call runs getSpecificItemCollection() which does Entry::whereItemId($statamic_id) (DB query, Availability.php line 338) and resolves rates via resolveRateForResult()/buildRatesAvailabilityCollection() executing Rate::forEntry(...)->published()->...->get() (lines 391/418). The entry row and the published rate set are identical across all periods (only dates change), yet they are re-queried 2*extraDays+1 times. With extraDays=7 that is 15× redundant Entry + Rate(+entries pivot) queries per search. Confirmed; medium.
  - **Fix:** Resolve the Entry row and the entry's published rate set once before the per-period loop and pass them into the per-period availability resolution, or memoize on the Availability instance keyed by statamic_id so repeated getAvailabilityForEntry calls within one request reuse them. The codebase already uses per-instance memoization (Rate's entry collection cache, HandlesPricing::$cachedRate), so the pattern is established.
  - **Evidence:** HandlesAvailabilityQueries.php lines 83-88: `$this->generateDatePeriods($this->data)->map(function ($period) { ... app(Availability::class)->getAvailabilityForEntry($searchData, $this->entryId, expireReservations: false, ...); })`. Availability.php line 338 `$resrvEntry = Entry::whereItemId($statamic_id);`, line 391 `Rate::forEntry($entry->item_id)->published()->with('entries')->get()`, line 418 `Rate::forEntry($entry->item_id)->published()->get()`.
  - _performance · confirmed · high confidence_

- [x] **M4 — Browse availability path runs a per-(item×rate) max_available check that issues reservation queries in a loop**
  - **Where:** `src/Models/Availability.php:290-331, 472-493`
  - **Problem:** getAvailabilityCollection() (the multi-entry browse path) groups by statamic_id and, per item, per candidate base/shared rate, calls ratePassesRestrictions() (472-479) which calls rateHasCapacity() (481-493). For shared rates with max_available, rateHasCapacity() calls AvailabilityRepository::checkMaxAvailable() -> validateMaxAvailable() -> validateMaxAvailableForDateRange(), which fires Rate::withoutGlobalScopes()->find() plus TWO reservation overlap queries (Reservation + ChildReservation, lines 371-387). So browsing M entries each with K capped shared rates issues ~M×K×(1 + 2) extra queries. The single-item showAllRates path uses the batched getExhaustedDatesForRates() (Availability.php line 870) which collapses to 2 queries, but the multi-entry browse path does not. Confirmed; medium is appropriate since it only bites when shared+max_available rates are configured across many browsed entries.
  - **Fix:** Hoist a single getExhaustedDatesForRates() call (it already accepts a collection of rates and returns exhausted dates keyed by rate id) out of the per-item/per-rate loop in getAvailabilityCollection(), then test date membership in-memory in place of the per-rate checkMaxAvailable() call inside ratePassesRestrictions/rateHasCapacity for this path. That turns M×K×3 queries into ~2 for the whole search.
  - **Evidence:** Availability.php lines 297, 310, 317 each call $this->ratePassesRestrictions($rate) inside the per-item foreach over rates. ratePassesRestrictions (472-479) ends with $this->rateHasCapacity($rate). rateHasCapacity (487-492) calls checkMaxAvailable per rate. AvailabilityRepository validateMaxAvailableForDateRange (371-387) runs two get() overlap queries. The batched alternative getExhaustedDatesForRates is used at Availability.php:870 (showAllRates path) but not in getAvailabilityCollection.
  - _performance · confirmed · high confidence_

- [x] **M5 — getExhaustedDatesForRates loads ALL non-terminal reservations with no date-range filter**
  - **Where:** `src/Repositories/AvailabilityRepository.php:319-360`
  - **Problem:** Confirmed. getExhaustedDatesForRates() fetches every non-terminal Reservation and ChildReservation for the shared rate IDs across all time with no date_start/date_end bound (lines 329-335), then expands each reservation's full CarbonPeriod into $dateCounts (lines 347-353) before filtering. It is invoked per availability search/calendar render from getAvailabilityCalendar() (line 718, via getExhaustedDatesForRate), getAvailableDatesFromDate() (line 787) and expandRatesFromBaseResults() (line 870). On a site with a long booking history on a shared rate, every search loads the entire reservation history for that rate into memory. The reviewer's note that expandRatesFromBaseResults() already computes $rangeStart/$rangeEnd (lines 874-876) but does NOT pass them down is accurate, so the bounding window is readily available. Contrast validateMaxAvailableForDateRange() (lines 371-387) which DOES bound by `date_start < dateEnd AND date_end > dateStart` — proving the unbounded query here is an oversight, not a deliberate design.
  - **Fix:** Add a date-range parameter to getExhaustedDatesForRates()/getExhaustedDatesForRate() and bound both reservation queries with `->where('date_start','<',$rangeEnd)->where('date_end','>',$rangeStart)` (mirroring validateMaxAvailableForDateRange line 374-375 / 384-385). expandRatesFromBaseResults already has $rangeStart/$rangeEnd; pass them through. The calendar/available-dates callers can derive the window from the rendered range.
  - **Evidence:** Lines 329-331: `Reservation::whereIn('rate_id', $rateIds)->whereNotIn('status', ReservationStatus::terminal())->get(['rate_id','quantity','date_start','date_end'])` — no date bound. Lines 347-353 expand every reservation's full CarbonPeriod. validateMaxAvailableForDateRange (line 374-375) shows the bounded pattern `->where('date_start','<',$dateEnd)->where('date_end','>',$dateStart)` is used elsewhere. expandRatesFromBaseResults computes `$rangeStart = $dates->min(); $rangeEnd = $dates->max();` (875-876) but never passes them into getExhaustedDatesForRates (line 870).
  - _performance · confirmed · high confidence_

- [x] **M6 — ResrvSearch scope returns ALL entries (unfiltered) when availability throws**
  - **Where:** `src/Scopes/ResrvSearch.php:29-32`
  - **Problem:** When a frontend collection search (the `resrv_search` query scope used by the lf-availability-filter Livewire filter) produces an AvailabilityException, the entire collection is shown as bookable instead of zero results. The chain is verifiable: initiateAvailability() (HandlesAvailabilityDates.php:93-115) throws AvailabilityException for past dates, pickup-after-dropoff, too-long/too-short stays, quantity over maximum, and lead-time violations. getAvailable() lets it propagate to HandlesAvailabilityQueries::getAvailability() (lines 36-44), whose catch returns an array containing only 'message' and 'request' keys — NO 'data' key. AvailabilityResource::toArray() ALWAYS includes a 'data' key (line 23), so the scope's guard `! isset($result['data']) && $result['message']['status'] === false` is reachable ONLY via this exception path, and it does `return $query` with no whereIn('id', …) constraint — leaking every entry. The normal 'nothing available' path is fine: getAvailabilityCollection() returns an empty-but-present data collection, so execution reaches line 36 and correctly yields whereIn('id', []) (verified by the passing test_it_returns_nothing_for_7_days). The inline `// TODO: throw an exception here` confirms the spot was left unfinished. Recalibrated to medium: the consequence (entire collection appears bookable) is severe, but it requires the visitor to submit an out-of-range/invalid search, and there is no test for this path.
  - **Fix:** On the no-data/error branch, exclude everything instead of returning the unfiltered query: `return $query->whereIn('id', []);`. Better, have getAvailability() signal the failure explicitly (or always return a 'data' key) so the scope can distinguish 'invalid search' from 'no availability'. Add a scope test that submits a too-long / past-date search and asserts 0 results.
  - **Evidence:** ResrvSearch.php:30-32 `if (! isset($result['data']) && $result['message']['status'] === false) { return $query; }`. HandlesAvailabilityQueries.php:36-44 returns `['message' => ['status' => false, 'error' => …], 'request' => $searchData]` (no 'data'). AvailabilityResource.php:22-23 always emits `'data' => $this->availability`. HandlesAvailabilityDates.php:32-37, 59-61, 99-104 throw AvailabilityException on out-of-range input. ResrvProvider.php:106 registers ResrvSearch as a scope; LfAvailabilityFilter.php:57 sets modifier 'resrv_search'.
  - _bug · confirmed · high confidence_

### Lifecycle (events / listeners / jobs)

- [x] **M7 — Imported price/available values are upserted without validation or numeric coercion**
  - **Where:** `src/Jobs/ProcessDataImport.php:100-138`
  - **Problem:** `$data['price']` and `$data['available']` originate from raw CSV cells (DataImport::prepare pushes `$value` and `$row[next column]` verbatim, DataImport.php:70-71) and are written via `Availability::upsert(...)` (Jobs/ProcessDataImport.php:120/124/138). `upsert()` bypasses Eloquent casts/mutators, so no coercion or validation occurs: a non-numeric price, negative `available`, or blank cell is written straight to `resrv_availabilities`/`resrv_rate_prices`. There is no validation anywhere in DataImport or the job (the only guard is the rate_id-required Log::warning at lines 65-66). Bad cells silently corrupt pricing/inventory.
  - **Fix:** Validate each row before upsert (numeric price >= 0, integer available >= 0, parseable dates) and skip+log invalid rows, mirroring the existing Log::warning pattern. Explicitly cast `(float)`/`(int)` the values.
  - **Evidence:** Jobs/ProcessDataImport.php:104-106 builds upsert rows with `'price' => $data['price'], 'available' => $data['available']` straight from CSV; line 120 `Availability::upsert($dataToAdd, ...)` and line 138 likewise. DataImport.php:70-71 `$arrayToPush['available'] = $row[...]; $arrayToPush['price'] = $value;` are unvalidated cell values. No validation step exists in either file.
  - _correctness · confirmed · high confidence_

### Pricing & Money

- [x] **M8 — calculateReservationTotals runs availability/pricing queries on every render**
  - **Where:** `src/Livewire/Traits/HandlesPricing.php:14-33`
  - **Problem:** calculateReservationTotals() is bound unconditionally in the checkout sidebar (checkout.blade.php:67 `:totals="$this->calculateReservationTotals()"`, inside the always-rendered sidebar div at lines 52-70, not gated by step). It is not memoised. Line 21 calls getUpdatedPrices(), which for a normal reservation runs Availability::getPricing() — a real DB query via AvailabilityRepository::itemPricesBetween() (Availability.php:131-137). For a PARENT reservation getUpdatedPricesForParent() (HandlesReservationQueries.php:198-204) loops every child issuing one getPricing() per child. So every Livewire render (each step transition, coupon change, gateway pick, etc.) re-runs these queries, N per render for multi-child carts, even though prices were already validated and persisted in step 1.
  - **Fix:** Memoise the recomputed prices for the request (private property or #[Computed]) or, for the sidebar display, read the already-persisted reservation price/payment/total and only recompute on coupon/extras changes.
  - **Evidence:** checkout.blade.php:67 calls $this->calculateReservationTotals() in the always-rendered sidebar. HandlesPricing.php:21 calls getUpdatedPrices(); HandlesReservationQueries.php:189 → Availability::getPricing() (DB query at Availability.php:131-137); getUpdatedPricesForParent (198-204) loops $this->reservation->childs with one getPricing per child.
  - _performance · confirmed · high confidence_

- [x] **M9 — No floor on price; fixed-decrease or >100% percent-decrease yields a negative price**
  - **Where:** `src/Models/DynamicPricing.php:219-249`
  - **Problem:** fixed() does `$price->subtract($amount)` for a 'decrease' with no lower bound, and percent() calls decreasePercent($amount). Price::decreasePercent (Price.php:68-74) computes `bcmul(100 - $percent, 0.01, 4)`; with amount=150 this is -0.5000, producing a negative Money (moneyphp permits negatives). So a misconfigured discount larger than the base price, or a percent decrease >100, flows through as a negative total/payment with no isNegative guard. Real, but the severity is gated by operator misconfiguration: the system already provides 'minimum'/'maximum' clamps (clampPolicies, fixed() minimum branch, and tested in DynamicPricingApplyTest test_fixed_minimum_*), so an operator who adds a minimum clamp is protected. There is no automatic floor and no CP validation preventing the misconfiguration, so medium is fair; treat as a hardening/validation gap rather than a guaranteed bug.
  - **Fix:** Floor the result at zero inside apply() (after clamps), e.g. `return $result->lessThan(Price::create(0)) ? Price::create(0) : $result;`, and/or validate at the CP that decrease amounts and percent decreases (0-100) cannot produce negatives.
  - **Evidence:** fixed() line 236 `return $price->subtract($amount);` with no floor; percent() line 222 `return $price->decreasePercent($policy->amount);`. decreasePercent multiplier reproduced: bcmul(100-150,0.01,4) = -0.5000. Minimum clamp exists (clampPolicies lines 200-205, fixed() minimum line 241-242) but is operator-optional.
  - _correctness · partially-confirmed · medium confidence_

- [x] **M10 — calculatePayment mutates the reservation Price in place; correctness depends on array evaluation order**
  - **Where:** `src/Traits/HandlesPricing.php:150-154`
  - **Problem:** For the 'percent' payment mode calculatePayment does `$price->percent(config('resrv-config.percent_amount'))` directly on the passed-in Price. Price::percent()/multiply() mutate $this->money and return $this (Price.php:46-66), so this rewrites the caller's reservationPrice to the deposit amount. The two call sites Availability.php:153-157 and :505-512 only stay correct because the array literal evaluates `'price' => $prices['reservationPrice']->format()` BEFORE `'payment' => $this->calculatePayment(...)->format()`. Reordering the keys, or reading reservationPrice again afterwards, would silently turn the displayed price into the deposit. The parallel code is consistently non-mutating: PaymentGatewayManager.php:206 and HandlesReservationQueries.php:122,217 all do `Price::create($x->format())->percent(...)`. calculatePayment is the outlier.
  - **Fix:** Make calculatePayment non-mutating like the siblings: `'percent' => Price::create($price->format())->percent(config('resrv-config.percent_amount'))`, decoupling the result from array evaluation order.
  - **Evidence:** HandlesPricing.php:152 `'percent' => $price->percent(config('resrv-config.percent_amount'))`. Price::percent (line 60-66) calls multiply which sets `$this->money = ...; return $this;`. Call sites Availability.php:154 ('price' key) precede :156 ('payment' key). Contrast PaymentGatewayManager.php:206 / HandlesReservationQueries.php:122,217 which all wrap in `Price::create(...->format())` first.
  - _bug · confirmed · high confidence_

- [x] **M11 — N+1: resolveSharedIndependentPrices runs two queries per item on the multi-entry browse path**
  - **Where:** `src/Traits/HandlesPricing.php:94-119`
  - **Problem:** Confirmed. On the multi-entry browse path, getAvailabilityCollection() (Availability.php:290-331) groupBy('statamic_id') and per item calls populateAvailability() -> getPrices(). When the rate hasIndependentSharedPricing(), getPrices() (HandlesPricing.php:44-52) calls resolveSharedIndependentPrices(), which fires one RatePrice query (line 98-102) plus, when there are missing override dates and a base rate, one Availability query (line 113-118) — i.e. up to 2 extra queries per (item, shared-independent rate). Browsing N entries with such a rate produces ~2N extra queries. The calendar/available-dates paths DO batch this via loadRateOverridesForRates() (Availability.php:936-957, called from expandRatesFromBaseResults line 878), confirming batching exists elsewhere but not on the collection browse path. Severity medium is fair: it only triggers for the shared-independent-pricing rate type and only on the multi-entry list path.
  - **Fix:** In getAvailabilityCollection(), batch-load RatePrice overrides (and base-rate Availability prices) for all grouped statamic_ids once via the existing loadRateOverridesForRates() pattern, then pass the prefetched maps down through populateAvailability()/getPrices() so resolveSharedIndependentPrices() does no per-item queries.
  - **Evidence:** HandlesPricing.php:98 `RatePrice::where('rate_id', $rate->id)->where('statamic_id', $statamicId)...->get()` and line 113 `Availability::where('rate_id', $rate->base_rate_id)->where('statamic_id', $statamicId)...->get()` are both per single $statamicId. getAvailabilityCollection() (Availability.php:292) maps per grouped statamic_id calling populateAvailability -> getPrices (line 499). The calendar path's expandRatesFromBaseResults batches via loadRateOverridesForRates (Availability.php:878) which uses `whereIn('statamic_id', $statamicIds)` (line 949).
  - _performance · confirmed · high confidence_

### Extras / Options / Cutoff

- [x] **M12 — Required-extras enforcement includes unpublished (and soft-deleted) extras, blocking checkout**
  - **Where:** `src/Models/Extra.php:218-232`
  - **Problem:** scopeEntriesWithConditions() builds a raw DB::table('resrv_extras') join with no where('published', true) and (being a raw query) bypasses the SoftDeletes global scope. It feeds ExtraCondition::requiredExtrasForEntry() -> hasRequiredExtrasSelected(), the server-side required-extras gate used by Reservation::checkForRequiredExtras() (Reservation.php:437). The customer-facing list (Extra::scopeGetPriceForDates filters published=true at Extra.php:239, and Extras::extras) never shows unpublished/trashed extras, and toggleExtra() can only select extras present in $this->extras. So if an admin unpublishes (or the soft-delete edge) an extra that still carries a required condition row, the gate keeps requiring it while the customer cannot select it, permanently blocking checkout with an unactionable 'ID X required...' message.
  - **Fix:** Add ->where('resrv_extras.published', true) and ->whereNull('resrv_extras.deleted_at') to the join in scopeEntriesWithConditions so the required-extras gate only considers extras the customer can actually see and select.
  - **Evidence:** Extra.php:223-231 DB::table('resrv_extras')->join(...resrv_entry_extra...)->join(...resrv_extra_conditions...)->select('resrv_extras.*','resrv_extra_conditions.*') with no published/deleted_at filter. Contrast Extra.php:239 scopeGetPriceForDates ->where('published', true). ExtraCondition.php:43 entriesWithConditions()->get() then filters operation=='required'. Confirmed required path is live: test_it_handles_required_extra passed (OK, 7 assertions).
  - _bug · confirmed · medium confidence_

- [x] **M13 — Option::calculatePrice null-derefs when a selected option value was soft-deleted**
  - **Where:** `src/Models/Option.php:52-57`
  - **Problem:** Option::calculatePrice($data,$value) does $value = $this->values->find($value); return $value->calculatePrice($data). values() is a plain hasMany and OptionValue uses SoftDeletes, and it is eager-loaded via $with=['values'] respecting the soft-delete scope, so a soft-deleted value is absent and find() returns null -> 'calculatePrice() on null'. This is reachable from Reservation::extraCharges() (Option.php:232) used by amountRemaining (Reservation.php:213), and from validateExtraCharges() (Reservation.php:389, which uses Option::find — not withTrashed). The reservation->options() relation withTrashed() (Reservation.php:152) only un-trashes the Option, not the OptionValue. CORRECTION to the original finding: the CP show endpoint does NOT 500 — ReservationCpController.php:147-154 uses values->firstWhere() with safe null navigation ($value?->name). The crash is confined to the pricing/charge paths (extraCharges/validateExtraCharges), and requires a historical reservation whose pivot value id has since been soft-deleted.
  - **Fix:** Look up the value tolerating trashed rows where a reservation references it: $value = $this->values()->withTrashed()->find($value); and guard null before calling calculatePrice (e.g. return Price::create(0) or load values withTrashed for reservation pricing). Also use Option::withTrashed() consistently in validateExtraCharges (line 389) for the non-parent path.
  - **Evidence:** Option.php:54-56 $value=$this->values->find($value); return $value->calculatePrice($data). Option.php:39 values()=hasMany; OptionValue.php:16 uses SoftDeletes; Option.php:25 $with=['values']. Reservation.php:152 options() withTrashed (Option only). ReservationCpController.php:152-154 safe nav $value?->name, so display path does not crash.
  - _bug · partially-confirmed · medium confidence_

- [x] **M14 — Cutoff validation throws false error when a date has no matching schedule and no default**
  - **Where:** `src/Traits/HandlesCutoffRules.php:44-49`
  - **Problem:** When enable_cutoff_rules is on and enable_cutoff is true for the entry but no schedule matches the date and no default_starting_time/default_cutoff_hours is set, getCutoffScheduleForDate() returns a TRUTHY array ['starting_time'=>null,'cutoff_hours'=>null,'schedule_name'=>'No Schedule Provided']. HandlesCutoffValidation::validateCutoffRules() only skips on `! $schedule` (line 22), so it proceeds to isWithinCutoffWindow() with nulls: Carbon::parse($date.' '.null) yields the date at 00:00 and subHours(null) subtracts 0, giving a cutoff of the date's midnight. I reproduced that Carbon::now() (today) greaterThan that midnight => true, so a CutoffException is thrown for a same-day/started date with a message interpolating null :hours/:time. The 'No Schedule Provided' label clearly means 'no cutoff applies', so it must not block. Reachability requires this specific misconfiguration (feature on, entry opted in, no matching schedule, no default).
  - **Fix:** Either return null from getCutoffScheduleForDate() when neither a matching schedule nor a default exists, or in validateCutoffRules()/isWithinCutoffWindow() treat a null starting_time or null cutoff_hours as 'no cutoff' and return without throwing.
  - **Evidence:** HandlesCutoffRules.php:44-48 returns the array with null starting_time/cutoff_hours and schedule_name 'No Schedule Provided'. HandlesCutoffValidation.php:22 `if (! $schedule) return;` does not catch a truthy-but-null-valued array. Repro: startingDateTime 2026-05-29 00:00:00, cutoffTime 2026-05-29 00:00:00, now greaterThan => true.
  - _bug · confirmed · high confidence_

### CP / HTTP & Routing

- [x] **M15 — Data import 'store' is a state-mutating GET that processes a globally-cached uploaded CSV**
  - **Where:** `routes/cp.php:81`
  - **Problem:** Route `Route::get('/resrv/dataimport/store', 'DataImportCpController@store')` (routes/cp.php:81) performs a state-mutating action via GET: store() dispatches ProcessDataImport (DataImportCpController.php:62-73), which writes availability/prices from the cached CSV into the DB. GET routes are CSRF-exempt, so a CP user could be CSRF-baited into triggering an import. The import object is cached under a single global key `resrv-data-import` (lines 18, 51, 64) and the upload is written to a fixed path `resrv-data-import/resrv-data-import.csv` (line 43, no per-user/random component), so two admins importing concurrently — or an attacker who can confirm() a file then have a victim hit store() — can cross-apply one user's file/collection under another's action. Combined with finding #1 (no `use resrv` gate), any `access cp` user can confirm+store arbitrary CSV into the availability tables. Medium: requires an authenticated CP account and the cross-user race is a narrow window, but it mutates pricing/availability data with no CSRF protection.
  - **Fix:** Change the store route to POST so CSRF protection applies (and update the Inertia call in resources/js/pages/DataImport to POST). Scope the cache key and stored filename per authenticated user (include the user id or a random token returned by confirm() and echoed back by store()). Re-validate the cached DataImport's collection at store() time. Also apply the `use resrv` gate from finding #1.
  - **Evidence:** routes/cp.php:81 `Route::get('/resrv/dataimport/store', ...)`. DataImportCpController.php:43 `$file->storeAs('resrv-data-import', 'resrv-data-import.csv')` (fixed path), 51 `Cache::put('resrv-data-import', $dataImport)` (global key), 64 `Cache::has('resrv-data-import')`, 68 `ProcessDataImport::dispatch()`.
  - _security · confirmed · medium confidence_

- [x] **M16 — Data import uses a fixed file name and cache key — concurrent imports clobber each other; store() is a GET that mutates data**
  - **Where:** `src/Http/Controllers/DataImportCpController.php:43-51, 62-68`
  - **Problem:** confirm() stores the upload at the constant path `resrv-data-import/resrv-data-import.csv` (line 43) and caches the DataImport under the constant key `resrv-data-import` (line 51; also forgotten in index() at line 18). store() (lines 62-68) checks/consumes that single cache key and dispatches ProcessDataImport. Two concurrent CP imports overwrite each other's file and cache, so the second user's data silently replaces the first's before store() runs. Additionally store() is registered as `Route::get('/resrv/dataimport/store', ...)` (routes/cp.php:81) — a state-mutating, queue-dispatching action behind a GET (prefetchable, CSRF-exempt, violates HTTP semantics). Both halves confirmed; medium is right.
  - **Fix:** Namespace the temp file and cache key per authenticated user/session (e.g. include `Statamic\Facades\User::current()->id()` or a random token returned to the client), and change the store route to POST.
  - **Evidence:** DataImportCpController.php:43 `$path = $file->storeAs('resrv-data-import', 'resrv-data-import.csv');`, :51 `Cache::put('resrv-data-import', $dataImport);`, :64 `if (! Cache::has('resrv-data-import'))`, :68 `ProcessDataImport::dispatch();`. routes/cp.php:81 `Route::get('/resrv/dataimport/store', 'DataImportCpController@store')`.
  - _bug · confirmed · high confidence_

- [x] **M17 — Export CSV stream re-queries childs (with rate) per parent reservation row**
