### Entry mirror / Multisite

- [ ] **N22 — syncToDatabase ignores per-localization disabled state in multisite**
  - **Where:** `src/Models/Entry.php:58-85`
  - **Problem:** syncToDatabase returns early for any entry with an origin (if ($entry->hasOrigin()) return; - line 64), so only the origin's resrv_availability value drives the mirror's enabled flag (line 74) and the cached getDisabledIds() list. A localization can set its own resrv_availability to 'disabled', but that is never reflected in filtering. This is consistent with the addon's deliberate origin-scoped availability model (the whole multisite design maps localized ids back to the origin - see MultisiteAvailabilityTest), so it is almost certainly by design rather than a bug; the only risk is editor surprise if they expect to disable a single locale and it silently has no effect. Recalibrated to nit/by-design - a documentation or CP-UX clarification, not a code defect.
  - **Fix:** No code change needed if origin-scoped availability is intended (it clearly is). Document that availability/disable is origin-scoped, or hide/disable the resrv_availability disable toggle on localizations in the CP so the no-op is not surprising. Only if per-locale disabling is a real requirement would getDisabledIds resolution need to consider the localized field value.
  - **Evidence:** `if ($entry->hasOrigin()) { return; }` (Entry.php:64) precedes the mirror upsert that sets `'enabled' => $entry->get($field->handle()) !== 'disabled'` (line 74). getDisabledIds() reads the mirror's enabled flag only (lines 117-124). Origin-scoped design is corroborated throughout MultisiteAvailabilityTest.
  - _bug · partially-confirmed · medium confidence_

- [ ] **N23 — TOCTOU race: active-reservation check is unlocked, so a reservation created between the check and EntryDeleted can be orphaned**
  - **Where:** `src/Support/ActiveReservationsGuard.php:16-19`
  - **Problem:** hasActiveReservationsForEntry runs a plain ->exists() with no row lock and no transaction spanning the EntryDeleting guard through the EntryDeleted availability wipe. In principle a PENDING reservation committed (frontend checkout, HandlesReservationQueries.php:77) in the window between the guard's exists() and EntryDeleted's hard delete could be left pointing at an item whose availability was wiped. In practice the window is the few microseconds inside a single Entry::delete() call within one request (EntryDeleting at Entry.php:258 -> EntryDeleted at Entry.php:285), and admin deletes are rare, so the practical risk is minimal. The observation is valid - the guard is best-effort, not atomic - but the original 'low' severity overstates it; nit is more accurate. No code change is strictly required.
  - **Fix:** Optional/document-only. If true atomicity is wanted, wrap the deleting check + availability cleanup in a transaction with a lockForUpdate on the item's reservations/availability, or add an advisory lock on the item id. At minimum add a comment that the guard is best-effort. Given the tiny same-request window, accepting and documenting the risk is reasonable.
  - **Evidence:** `return Reservation::where('item_id', $statamicId)->whereNotIn('status', ReservationStatus::terminal())->exists();` (lines 16-18) - no lockForUpdate, no surrounding transaction. EntryDeleting and EntryDeleted both fire inside one Entry::delete() (vendor Entry.php:258 and 285), so the window is intra-request.
  - _correctness · confirmed · medium confidence_

- [ ] **N24 — getDefaultSiteEntry throws a domain AvailabilityException for a generic 'entry not found' lookup**
  - **Where:** `src/Traits/HandlesMultisiteIds.php:13-17`
  - **Problem:** getDefaultSiteEntry is a generic multisite id resolver used by Availability, Extra, and Livewire components, yet on a missing entry it throws AvailabilityException('An entry with this ID cannot be found.'). Coupling a pure id-resolution helper to the availability domain means non-availability callers (e.g. a Livewire mount resolving an entry id) surface a misleading 'availability' error for what is really a not-found condition. Minor semantic smell; nit severity is correct. No functional bug.
  - **Fix:** Throw a neutral/dedicated exception (e.g. an EntryNotFoundException) or accept a nullable return so callers decide. At minimum reword the message so it is not availability-specific.
  - **Evidence:** `$entry = Entry::find($statamic_id); if (! $entry) { throw new AvailabilityException(__('An entry with this ID cannot be found.')); }` (lines 13-16); the import is `use Reach\StatamicResrv\Exceptions\AvailabilityException;` (line 5). Trait is named HandlesMultisiteIds and consumed broadly (Extra::scopeEntriesWithConditions:220, AvailabilityResults:70).
  - _best-practice · confirmed · high confidence_

### CP / HTTP & Routing

- [ ] **N25 — AffiliateCpController::delete returns response(200) which sets '200' as the body, not via a clear status**
  - **Where:** `src/Http/Controllers/AffiliateCpController.php:92`
  - **Problem:** `return response(200);` (AffiliateCpController.php:92) passes 200 as the response content (body becomes the string '200') with a default 200 status. It works but is misleading and inconsistent with the JSON responses used elsewhere in the controller. Additionally, the Affiliate model uses SoftDeletes (Affiliate.php:13), so `$affiliate->delete()` (line 86) soft-deletes, while the pivot cleanup (lines 88-90) hard-deletes `resrv_reservation_affiliate` rows — an inconsistency worth a comment (the soft-deleted affiliate is detached from its reservations' fee history).
  - **Fix:** Return `response()->noContent()` (204) or `response()->json([], 200)` to make the status explicit; optionally document the soft-delete-vs-hard-delete-pivot intent.
  - **Evidence:** AffiliateCpController.php:92 `return response(200);`. Line 86 `$affiliate->delete();` on a model with `use HasFactory, SoftDeletes;` (Affiliate.php:13). Lines 88-90 `DB::table('resrv_reservation_affiliate')->where('affiliate_id', $affiliate->id)->delete();` hard-deletes pivot rows.
  - _best-practice · confirmed · high confidence · also independently flagged by: cp-controllers sweep(s)_

- [ ] **N26 — ExtraCpController::entryIndex / ExtraCpCategoryController::entryIndex eager-resolve enabled flag with per-extra relation access**
  - **Where:** `src/Http/Controllers/ExtraCpController.php:31-41`
  - **Problem:** ExtraCpController::entryIndex eager-loads `$this->extra->with('entries')->get()` then per extra runs `$extra->entries->contains($entry)` in memory — not a query-level N+1, as the reviewer concedes. ExtraCpCategoryController::entryIndex (lines 46-64) eager-loads `extras.entries` for every category (and separately for uncategorized), materializing the full entry pivot set for all extras just to compute a boolean `enabled` flag. On installs with many entry associations this hydrates large pivot collections into memory. This is an efficiency observation, not a bug; acceptable for small datasets. Confidence/severity recalibrated to nit — the reviewer themselves rated it low confidence and there is no correctness problem.
  - **Fix:** Optional: compute the enabled set once for the target entry via a single pivot query (select extra_ids associated with this entry), then map booleans, instead of hydrating `extras.entries` for all categories. Only worth doing if profiling shows it matters.
  - **Evidence:** ExtraCpController.php:34-38 `$extras = $this->extra->with('entries')->get(); $extras->each(function ($extra) use ($entry) { $extra->setAttribute('enabled', $extra->entries->contains($entry)); });`. ExtraCpCategoryController.php:46-55 `$this->category->with('extras', 'extras.entries')->get()->transform(...)` then per extra `$extra->entries->contains($entry)`. Relations are eager-loaded (no per-row query); the cost is memory of hydrated pivots.
  - _performance · partially-confirmed · medium confidence_

- [ ] **N27 — RateCpController::indexCp dereferences ->first()['handle'] when no resrv collections exist**
  - **Where:** `src/Http/Controllers/RateCpController.php:25-26`
  - **Problem:** `$selectedCollection = $request->query('collection', $collections->first()['handle'] ?? null);` (line 26). collectionsWithResrv() returns a Statamic Collection of arrays; when empty, `->first()` is null, and `null['handle']` emits a PHP 8 warning 'Trying to access array offset on value of type null' before the `?? null` resolves the expression to null. The page still renders (no fatal). Real but cosmetic — recalibrated from low to nit: it is a non-fatal warning on a fresh install with zero resrv-enabled collections, surfaced only when the user has not passed a `?collection=` query param.
  - **Fix:** Compute defensively: `$first = $collections->first(); $selectedCollection = $request->query('collection', $first['handle'] ?? null);`
  - **Evidence:** RateCpController.php:25-26 `$collections = ResrvHelper::collectionsWithResrv()->values(); $selectedCollection = $request->query('collection', $collections->first()['handle'] ?? null);`. ResrvHelper::collectionsWithResrv() maps to `['title' => ..., 'handle' => ...]` arrays, so `->first()` on an empty set is null and `null['handle']` warns in PHP 8.x.
  - _bug · partially-confirmed · medium confidence_

- [ ] **N28 — resrv_rates_exist cached forever but only invalidated on create/delete, not restore in all paths**
  - **Where:** `src/Resources/ReservationResource.php:79-81`
  - **Problem:** ReservationResource::setColumns() uses Cache::rememberForever('resrv_rates_exist', fn () => Rate::withoutGlobalScopes()->exists()). This is a sound caching choice (avoids an exists() query per list render). The finding itself acknowledges this is not a perf bug — it is a maintainability/correctness fragility note: a rememberForever key with manual invalidation will leave the `rate` column wrongly hidden/shown until cache clear if any future path creates the first rate or trashes the last one without Cache::forget('resrv_rates_exist'). Restore-from-trash in particular is a path that may not forget the key. Correct as a nit; category is maintainability rather than performance.
  - **Fix:** Either bound staleness with Cache::remember(..., now()->addMinutes(10), ...), or (better) add a Rate model observer/booted() that forgets 'resrv_rates_exist' on created/deleted/restored so every mutation path is covered centrally instead of relying on each controller to remember.
  - **Evidence:** Lines 79-81: `if (! Cache::rememberForever('resrv_rates_exist', fn () => Rate::withoutGlobalScopes()->exists())) { unset($columns['rate']); }`. rememberForever + manual invalidation is inherently fragile for the restore path.
  - _maintainability · confirmed · medium confidence_

### Frontend Livewire

- [ ] **N29 — updateRateQuantity has no upper bound, allowing arbitrarily large per-rate quantities**
  - **Where:** `src/Livewire/AvailabilityMultiResults.php:169-172`
  - **Problem:** updateRateQuantity(int $rateId, int $quantity) only clamps the lower bound: `$this->rateQuantities[$rateId] = max(0, $quantity);` (line 171). No upper clamp and no check that $rateId exists in entryRates/availability, so a client can set huge quantities or pollute the rateQuantities map with arbitrary keys. UX/defensive gap only: maximum_quantity and per-rate availability are enforced server-side in validateMultiAvailabilityAndPrice() at checkout, and addSelections() skips rate IDs not present in availability (line 191). No overbooking or money bypass; arbitrary keys merely bloat the bound array harmlessly. Confirmed at nit severity.
  - **Fix:** Clamp the upper bound and ignore unknown rate IDs: `if (! isset($this->entryRates[$rateId])) { return; } $this->rateQuantities[$rateId] = max(0, min($quantity, config('resrv-config.maximum_quantity')));`.
  - **Evidence:** Lines 169-172: `public function updateRateQuantity(int $rateId, int $quantity): void { $this->rateQuantities[$rateId] = max(0, $quantity); }`. addSelections 189-193 guards `$rateData = $this->availability->get($rateId); if (! $rateData || data_get($rateData,'message.status') !== true) { continue; }`. validateMultiAvailabilityAndPrice 151-157 enforces maximum_quantity at checkout.
  - _best-practice · confirmed · high confidence_

- [ ] **N30 — Hardcoded non-translated 'Rate' fallback label for cart selections**
  - **Where:** `src/Livewire/AvailabilityMultiResults.php:201`
  - **Problem:** addSelections() stores `'rate_label' => $this->entryRates[$rateId] ?? 'Rate'` (line 201). The fallback 'Rate' is hardcoded English and not passed through the translation layer, unlike other user-facing strings in the component which use __(). It is rendered directly in availability-multi-results.blade.php line 95. Pure style nit, confirmed.
  - **Fix:** Wrap the fallback in the translation helper: `$this->entryRates[$rateId] ?? __('statamic-resrv::frontend.rate')` and add the key to the language files (matching the addon's translation namespace convention).
  - **Evidence:** Line 201: `'rate_label' => $this->entryRates[$rateId] ?? 'Rate',`. availability-multi-results.blade.php line 95: `<div class="font-medium">{{ $selection['rate_label'] }} × {{ $selection['quantity'] }}</div>`.
  - _style · confirmed · high confidence_

- [ ] **N31 — Null-deref fallback in getExtrasForReservation/getOptionsForReservation is broken**
  - **Where:** `src/Livewire/Traits/HandlesExtrasQueries.php:16`
  - **Problem:** `$reservation = $this->reservation ?? Reservation::findOrFail($this->reservation->id);` (HandlesExtrasQueries.php:16, identical at HandlesOptionsQueries.php:15). If the left operand were ever null, the right operand dereferences $this->reservation->id on that same null, throwing rather than falling back. In practice this is dead/latent: in Checkout, $this->reservation is a #[Computed] (getReservation) that never returns null (it throws), and in Extras/Options it is a non-nullable typed property. So the fallback can never do anything useful and only obscures intent. Nit, not low — there is no reachable failure, just confusing dead code.
  - **Fix:** Drop the unreachable fallback: `$reservation = $this->reservation;`. If a fallback is genuinely wanted, fetch by session id, not by $this->reservation->id.
  - **Evidence:** HandlesExtrasQueries.php:16 and HandlesOptionsQueries.php:15. $this->reservation is the Checkout #[Computed] (Checkout.php:116-120 → getReservation throws, never returns null) or a typed non-null property on Extras (Extras.php:31-32) / Options.
  - _bug · confirmed · high confidence_

### Vue / CP UI

- [ ] **N32 — Clipboard copy gives a success toast even if writeText rejects**
  - **Where:** `resources/js/components/AffiliatesList.vue:100-108`
  - **Problem:** copyLink (lines 100-108) calls `navigator.clipboard.writeText(link)` and immediately calls `toast.success('Affiliate link copied to clipboard')` without awaiting the returned promise. writeText is async and can reject (permission denied, document not focused, blocked context). On rejection the user sees a false 'copied' message plus an unhandled promise rejection. The else branch only handles the case where `navigator.clipboard` is entirely absent, not a rejected write. Correctly scoped nit.
  - **Fix:** Await the promise and branch on outcome: `navigator.clipboard.writeText(link).then(() => toast.success(__('Affiliate link copied to clipboard'))).catch(() => toast.error(__('Failed to copy link. Are you using SSL?')));`
  - **Evidence:** Lines 102-107: `if (navigator.clipboard) { navigator.clipboard.writeText(link); toast.success('Affiliate link copied to clipboard'); } else { toast.error('Failed to copy link...'); }`. The success toast fires synchronously regardless of whether writeText resolves. Confirmed.
  - _best-practice · confirmed · high confidence_

- [ ] **N33 — Untranslated user-facing strings in toasts**
  - **Where:** `resources/js/components/AffiliatesList.vue:104,106,125,130`
  - **Problem:** Several toast strings in AffiliatesList.vue are hardcoded English without the `__()` helper that the rest of the component uses (e.g. line 4 `__('Add a new affiliate')`, line 143 in AffiliatesPanel `__('Affiliate successfully saved')`): line 104 'Affiliate link copied to clipboard', line 106 'Failed to copy link. Are you using SSL?', line 125 'Affiliate deleted', line 130 'Cannot delete affiliate'. The count-error toast at line 203 ('Cannot retrieve reservation count') in ReservationsExport.vue and AffiliatesPanel.vue line 125 'Cannot retrieve the coupons' are similarly unwrapped. These break localization. Correctly a style nit.
  - **Fix:** Wrap each string in `__()`, e.g. `toast.success(__('Affiliate deleted'))`, for consistency and translatability.
  - **Evidence:** Line 104: `toast.success('Affiliate link copied to clipboard')`; line 106: `toast.error('Failed to copy link. Are you using SSL?')`; line 125: `toast.success('Affiliate deleted')`; line 130: `toast.error('Cannot delete affiliate')` — none use `__()`, while line 4 and AffiliatesPanel line 143 do. AffiliatesPanel line 125 `toast.error('Cannot retrieve the coupons')` confirms the same gap. Confirmed.
  - _style · confirmed · high confidence_

- [ ] **N34 — percentage column can render NaN% / shows raw decimal precision**
  - **Where:** `resources/js/components/ReportsItemsTable.vue:40-42`
  - **Problem:** Two claims, with different validity. (1) NaN%: NOT currently reachable — the backend always sets `percentage` to a number. Report::topSellerItems/topSellerExtras (Report.php lines 61 and 77) always assign `round($item->occurrences / $this->countConfirmedReservations(), 2)`, a float. There is no code path producing null/undefined percentage, and the divisor cannot be 0 when items exist (topItems only exist when confirmed reservations exist). So `Math.round(item.percentage * 100)` never yields NaN with the current shape. (2) Precision loss IS real but minor: the server rounds to 2 decimals first, so any share below 0.5% collapses to 0% on screen (verified: PHP round(0.004,2)=0, round(0.005,2)=0.01). A true 0.4% item shows '0%'. This is a cosmetic precision quirk, not a correctness bug. Recalibrated to nit.
  - **Fix:** Optional hardening: `{{ item.percentage != null ? Math.round(item.percentage * 100) : 0 }}%`. To avoid the sub-0.5% collapse, return the percentage from the backend already scaled (e.g. `round($occurrences / $count * 100, 1)`) instead of rounding the fraction to 2 decimals first.
  - **Evidence:** Template lines 40-42: `{{ Math.round(item.percentage * 100) }}%`. Backend Report.php line 61: `'percentage' => round($item->occurrences / $this->countConfirmedReservations(), 2)` (and line 77 for extras) always produces a float. `php -r round()` shows 0.004→0, 0.005→0.01, confirming sub-0.5% shares display 0%. NaN claim refuted (no null path); precision-loss claim confirmed but cosmetic.
  - _correctness · partially-confirmed · high confidence_

- [ ] **N35 — FullCalendar options object is non-reactive; only onlyStart is wired**
  - **Where:** `resources/js/components/ReservationsCalendar.vue:63-93`
  - **Problem:** calendarOptions (lines 63-88) is a plain, non-reactive object bound to `<FullCalendar :options="calendarOptions" />` (line 12). The onlyStart toggle works only because events.extraParams is a function read at fetch time (lines 69-74) combined with an explicit `watch(onlyStart, () => calApi.refetchEvents())` (lines 90-93). This is correct today, but it is a subtle pattern: any future option that should react to component state (timeZone, a date-range prop, etc.) will silently not update because the object isn't reactive and the wrapper diffs the bound options object. Correctly scoped as a nit — documentation/robustness, not a bug.
  - **Fix:** Add a short comment explaining the function+watch pattern for onlyStart, or convert calendarOptions to a `computed`/`reactive` so the FullCalendar wrapper uniformly picks up reactive option changes.
  - **Evidence:** Lines 63-88 define `const calendarOptions = { ... events: { url, extraParams: () => onlyStart.value ? {onlyStart:1} : {} }, ... }` (plain object). Lines 90-93: `watch(onlyStart, () => { fullCalendarRef.value?.getApi()?.refetchEvents(); })`. The function-valued extraParams plus explicit refetch is the only thing making the toggle reactive. Confirmed subtle-pattern nit.
  - _Vue · confirmed · high confidence_

- [ ] **N36 — localStorage write watcher uses deep:true on an array of primitives**
  - **Where:** `resources/js/components/ReservationsExport.vue:154-160`
  - **Problem:** The selectedFields persistence watcher (lines 154-160) uses `{ deep: true }`, but selectedFields is always reassigned as a brand-new array of string keys: loadSelectedFields returns a new array (lines 165-179), toggleGroup reassigns `selectedFields.value = [...]` (lines 233, 237), and CheckboxGroup's v-model replaces the value. A shallow (default) watch already fires on each reassignment, so deep traversal of an array of primitives adds cost for no benefit. Correctly scoped as a nit. (Even in the unlikely case CheckboxGroup mutated in place, the array holds only primitives, so a shallow watch on reassignment is the documented/normal pattern here.)
  - **Fix:** Drop `{ deep: true }` — the default shallow watch fires on each reassignment, which is the only way selectedFields changes.
  - **Evidence:** Lines 154-160: `watch(selectedFields, (value) => { ... localStorage.setItem ... }, { deep: true });`. selectedFields is reassigned in loadSelectedFields (returns `.map(...)`, lines 178), toggleGroup (`selectedFields.value = ...`, lines 233/237). Array of strings + reassignment ⇒ deep:true is redundant. Confirmed nit.
  - _performance · confirmed · high confidence_

- [ ] **N37 — handleSuccess called with an argument it does not accept**
  - **Where:** `resources/js/composables/useFormHandler.js:14,41`
  - **Problem:** save() calls `.then((response) => handleSuccess(response.data))` (line 41) but handleSuccess() is declared with no parameters (line 14) and ignores any argument. Harmless but misleading — it suggests the response body is consumed when it is discarded.
  - **Fix:** Either drop the argument (`.then(() => handleSuccess())`) or accept and use it (`function handleSuccess(data) { ... }`) if a caller will need the response payload.
  - **Evidence:** useFormHandler.js:14 `function handleSuccess() {` (zero params); line 41 `.then((response) => handleSuccess(response.data))` passes response.data which is never read inside handleSuccess (lines 14-18 only set disableSave, toast, emit).
  - _style · confirmed · high confidence_

- [ ] **N38 — useToast relies on legacy instance proxy via getCurrentInstance**
  - **Where:** `resources/js/composables/useToast.js:1-9`
  - **Problem:** useToast() reads `const { proxy } = getCurrentInstance();` and returns closures over proxy.$toast. getCurrentInstance() returns null outside an active component setup (e.g. if a future caller invokes useToast lazily inside an async callback or a non-component module), which would throw 'Cannot destructure property proxy of null'. Statamic's own CreateForm.vue reads the same global the idiomatic Vue-3 way via `instance.appContext.config.globalProperties`. Today every resrv caller invokes useToast synchronously in setup so it works (proxy does proxy globalProperties in Vue 3), but it is brittle and inconsistent with core.
  - **Fix:** Resolve $toast from appContext.config.globalProperties with a null guard captured once: `const instance = getCurrentInstance(); const $toast = instance?.appContext.config.globalProperties.$toast;` and fail loudly if missing rather than throwing on `.proxy`.
  - **Evidence:** useToast.js:4 `const { proxy } = getCurrentInstance();` then 6-7 `success: (message) => proxy.$toast.success(message)`. vendor ui/CreateForm.vue:27 `const { $slug, $axios, $toast, $keys } = instance.appContext.config.globalProperties;` — core's idiomatic access. No null guard on getCurrentInstance() in useToast.
  - _best-practice · confirmed · medium confidence_

- [ ] **N39 — clearAvailability is dead code**

It also assigns availability.value = '' (an empty string) to a ref that elsewhere holds an availability object, matching the loose initial declaration `const availability = ref('')` on line 65, which is a type smell.
  - **Fix:** Remove clearAvailability() unless it is intended to be wired up (e.g. clear the calendar when reservations are disabled). For consistency initialize availability to {} instead of '' so renderDay / pendingByDateForSelection always index an object.

Line 65 `const availability = ref('');` while line 92 indexes it as an object `availability.value[key]`.

- [ ] **N40 — Unused Link import and unused indexUrl prop in DataImport/Confirm.vue**

Maintainability/UX nit.

- [ ] **N42 — Redundant v-if + :open on ConfirmationModal**

Purely cosmetic; no functional bug (cancelRefund/refund both null out refundId, so it does close).

- [ ] **N44 — Refund modal can be opened for non-refundable (terminal) reservations**
  - **Where:** `resources/js/pages/Reservations/Index.vue:51-64`
  - **Problem:** The finding's underlying concern is real but its framing is partly off. The server IS robust: ReservationCpController::refund() short-circuits with 409 if already refunded (lines 202-204) and 422 if the status cannot transition to REFUNDED (lines 206-209), confirmed by tests test_refund_on_already_refunded_reservation_short_circuits_before_gateway and test_refund_on_expired_reservation_is_rejected_before_gateway. So no double-refund or invalid transition can occur. The genuine (minor) issue is purely UX: the listing renders the Refund DropdownItem for every row with no per-status gating, so a user can open the modal and click Refund on an expired/refunded reservation, producing an avoidable failed request and an error toast. The refund() error branch (lines 59-61) correctly keeps the modal open and shows error?.response?.data?.error. This is a nit, not a correctness bug.
  - **Fix:** Gate the Refund DropdownItem (and confirmRefund) on a refundable status, mirroring the server: v-if="['confirmed','partner'].includes(reservation.status)". This removes avoidable failed requests; the server already enforces the invariant.
  - **Evidence:** refund() catch block (Index.vue:59-61): `toast.error(error?.response?.data?.error ?? __('Something went wrong'));` and refundId left set. Server gates: refund() lines 202-204 (409) and 206-209 (422). DropdownItem (line 116) has no status condition.
  - _best-practice · partially-confirmed · high confidence_

### Affiliate / Customer / Data / Misc

- [ ] **N45 — Customer::get() matches internal model properties via property_exists**
  - **Where:** `src/Models/Customer.php:40-50`
  - **Problem:** `get()` checks `property_exists($this, $key) || array_key_exists($key, $this->attributes)` (Customer.php:43). Eloquent attributes ('id','email','customer_id', etc.) are not real PHP object properties — they live in `$this->attributes` — so the `property_exists($this, $key)` clause only ever matches the model's internal protected properties ('table','casts','guarded','connection','attributes', etc.). For such a key it calls `getAttribute($key)`, returning null/unexpected rather than the intended data-collection lookup. The `array_key_exists($key, $this->attributes)` clause alone already covers the real columns, so the `property_exists` branch only adds a small surprise surface. Functionally harmless in practice (templates query real fields), hence nit.
  - **Fix:** Drop the `property_exists($this, $key)` clause and rely on `array_key_exists($key, $this->attributes)` (plus an explicit allow-list for 'id'/'email' if desired) before falling through to the data collection.
  - **Evidence:** Customer.php:43 `if (property_exists($this, $key) || array_key_exists($key, $this->attributes)) { return $this->getAttribute($key); }`. Eloquent stores columns in `$attributes`, not as declared properties, so `property_exists` matches only internal protected props like `$table` (line 19), `$guarded`, `$casts`.
  - _maintainability · confirmed · medium confidence_

### Mail / Support / Providers

- [ ] **N46 — Redundant manual command registration duplicates AddonServiceProvider::bootCommands()**
  - **Where:** `src/Providers/ResrvProvider.php:226-229`
  - **Problem:** bootAddon() adds `Artisan::starting(fn ($artisan) => $artisan->resolveCommands($this->commands));`. Statamic's AddonServiceProvider::boot() already chains ->bootCommands() (line 209) BEFORE ->bootAddon() (line 226), and bootCommands() does `$this->commands($commands)` with $this->commands merged with autoloaded Commands/ and Console/Commands/ folders. So $this->commands are registered twice. Harmless (command registration is idempotent) but redundant/confusing dead code. Confirmed as a nit.
  - **Fix:** Remove the Artisan::starting(...) block in bootAddon() and rely on the inherited bootCommands() registration of $this->commands.
  - **Evidence:** ResrvProvider.php lines 226-229: `Artisan::starting(function ($artisan) { $artisan->resolveCommands($this->commands); });`. vendor AddonServiceProvider.php boot() line 209 `->bootCommands()` then line 226 `->bootAddon()`; bootCommands() lines 410-418 `if ($this->app->runningInConsole()) { ... $this->commands($commands); }` where $commands merges $this->commands.
  - _maintainability · confirmed · high confidence_

### Database / Migrations

- [ ] **N47 — payment_surcharge stored as float column — rounding drift vs Price/integer-cents model**
  - **Where:** `database/migrations/2026_04_04_000000_add_payment_surcharge_to_resrv_reservations.php:12`
  - **Problem:** Confirmed the column is `float(8,2)`. However the finding's central claim that this 'diverges from how payment/price/total are stored' is factually wrong: price, payment and total are ALL declared `float(8,2)` in their migrations (2021_05_04 create_reservations and 2024_03_20 add_total). So payment_surcharge is consistent with the existing money columns, and the Price cast reads/writes via the decimal(2dp) string, with all arithmetic done in moneyphp integer minor units in PHP (Price::add at runtime, never on the raw float). The generic 'float for money is risky' caution is valid but is a pre-existing project-wide pattern, not a new divergence introduced here. Downgraded to a nit/consistency note; not actionable for this column alone without migrating all money columns.
  - **Fix:** If desired, migrate ALL monetary columns (price, payment, total, payment_surcharge) to decimal(10,2) or integer cents in one coordinated migration; otherwise no change needed for payment_surcharge specifically. Ensure (as is already the case) no float arithmetic is performed — values flow through Price/moneyphp.
  - **Evidence:** Migration line 12 `$table->float('payment_surcharge', 8, 2)->default(0)`. create_reservations:25-26 `$table->float('price',8,2); $table->float('payment',8,2);` and add_total:17 `$table->float('total',8,2)` — same type, refuting the 'diverges' claim. Reservation casts (38-41) cast all four to PriceClass; Price.php does arithmetic via moneyphp Money (integer minor units) and bcmul, not on floats.
  - _correctness · partially-confirmed · high confidence_

### Other

- [ ] **N48 — Coupon value rendered via x-html instead of x-text**
  - **Where:** `resources/views/livewire/components/checkout-coupon.blade.php:55`
  - **Problem:** Line 55 renders the applied coupon with `<span x-html="coupon" ...>` where coupon is the Alpine model bound to the raw text input (lines 3, 35). addCoupon() validates the code as alpha_dash (Checkout.php:524) and the chip only displays once applied===true (x-show on line 50, set on coupon-applied at line 19), so HTML cannot currently survive into this node — not exploitable today. But rendering a user-influenced string via x-html is a footgun: any future loosening of the coupon validation would turn it into self-XSS. Nit.
  - **Fix:** Use x-text="coupon" instead of x-html="coupon"; the coupon is plain text and never needs HTML interpretation.
  - **Evidence:** checkout-coupon.blade.php:55 `<span x-html="coupon" class="ml-3"></span>`; coupon bound to input via x-model (line 35). Server validation alpha_dash at Checkout.php:524.
  - _security · confirmed · high confidence_

- [ ] **N49 — AvailabilityField docblock annotation has a stray '(used)' token**
  - **Where:** `src/Facades/AvailabilityField.php:12`
  - **Problem:** Confirmed exactly as described. Line 12 reads `@method static void clearCacheForBlueprint(\Statamic\Fields\Blueprint $blueprint) (used)`. The trailing ` (used)` is not valid phpDoc and is clearly a leftover editing note; it pollutes the @method signature for IDEs/static analysis. Pure cosmetic nit.
  - **Fix:** Remove the trailing ` (used)` so the line reads `@method static void clearCacheForBlueprint(\Statamic\Fields\Blueprint $blueprint)`.
  - **Evidence:** AvailabilityField.php:12 `* @method static void clearCacheForBlueprint(\Statamic\Fields\Blueprint $blueprint) (used)` — the other three @method lines (9-11) have no such trailing token.
  - _style · confirmed · high confidence_

## Appendix A — Merged duplicate findings

These were reported by more than one sweep and collapsed into the primary item shown. Listed for completeness.

- **H2** ($appends=['entry'] forces a Statamic stache lookup per row, plus lazy rate/childs/customer N+1 in list & calendar) also covers:
  - xc-performance: $appends=['entry'] forces a Statamic Entry::find() per reservation on every serialization
  - xc-concurrency: Reservation appends 'entry' on every serialization, triggering a Statamic stache lookup + toAugmentedArray per model
- **H3** (ExpireReservations loads ALL pending reservations and runs synchronously on every availability search) also covers:
  - reservation-lifecycle: ExpireReservations loads ALL pending reservations and runs inline (incl. remote gateway cancels) on every front-end availability search
  - xc-concurrency: ExpireReservations loads ALL pending reservations unbounded and runs synchronously on every availability search
  - availability-core: Synchronous ExpireReservations on every search loads all PENDING reservations
- **H7** (Price::create hardcodes *100, breaking all non-2-decimal currencies (JPY, BHD, KWD, etc.)) also covers:
  - availability-core: Price::create hardcodes a 2-decimal subunit (bcmul $price * 100)
- **H9** (CP routes do not enforce the 'use resrv' permission — any CP user can refund payments, edit availability, delete data) also covers:
  - reservation-core: CP reservation routes (including refund) are not gated by the 'use resrv' permission
  - affiliate-customer-data: Resrv CP routes (data import, affiliates, availability, reservation refund) lack the 'use resrv' permission gate
  - xc-security: All Resrv CP routes except /export are missing the `use resrv` permission check
- **H11** (N+1 queries in the CP reservations listing (customer, extras, options, rate, childs.rate, entry per row)) also covers:
  - xc-performance: Reservation index endpoint has N+1 on rate/extras/options/entry for every row
- **H12** (Extra quantity has no server-side min/max validation, allowing negative quantities that reduce the amount charged) also covers:
  - extras-options: Negative / zero / over-maximum extra quantity is never validated server-side
- **M1** (Stripe webhook timestamp tolerance disabled — replay attacks possible) also covers:
  - xc-security: Stripe webhook signature verification runs with timestamp tolerance disabled (replay window)
- **M20** (Calendar endpoint loads all confirmed reservations in range with no eager loading or pagination (N+1)) also covers:
  - xc-performance: Reservation calendar lazy-loads rate label and childs per event
- **M22** (N+1 (NxM) queries when recalculating extras/options pricing for cart selections) also covers:
  - xc-performance: AvailabilityMultiResults recalculation re-fetches each Extra/Option once per cart selection
- **M25** (ReservationCreated side effects are not transactional with reservation creation — a thrown AvailabilityException leaves an orphan PENDING reservation) also covers:
  - xc-concurrency: Reservation row is committed before availability is decremented, leaving orphaned PENDING rows on a lost decrement race
  - livewire-availability: Multi-cart reservation is committed before availability is decremented, leaving orphaned rows on concurrent overbooking
- **M26** (ExtraConditionsForm aliases and mutates the parent extra's nested conditions array (prop mutation)) also covers:
  - vue-fieldtypes-composables: ExtraConditionsForm mutates the data prop in place
- **M35** (Report::topSellerItems triggers N+1 entry lookups and re-filters/re-sums the full collection per item) also covers:
  - affiliate-customer-data: Report appends 'entry' triggers a Statamic Entry::find per row
- **L1** (Confirmed/terminal short-circuits run before signature verification (pre-auth DB probe)) also covers:
  - xc-concurrency: Stripe webhook runs DB lookups and entry/stache reads on attacker-controlled input before signature verification
- **L2** (Dead/duplicated pre-verification Event::constructFrom on the unverified payload) also covers:
  - xc-security: verifyPayment decodes/constructs the event payload twice; first parse is unverified and discarded
- **L3** (Stripe signature header read via raw $_SERVER superglobal, breaking on missing header) also covers:
  - xc-security: Stripe signature header read with undefined-index risk
  - xc-concurrency: Webhook reads $_SERVER['HTTP_STRIPE_SIGNATURE'] directly instead of the request
- **L10** (transitionTo() can throw InvalidStateTransition under a status race; webhook/Checkout callers don't catch it) also covers:
  - xc-concurrency: expire/confirm race can throw uncaught InvalidStateTransition inside the Stripe webhook, returning 500 and forcing a Stripe retry
- **L12** (Unrestricted mass assignment ($guarded = []) on Reservation and ChildReservation) also covers:
  - xc-security: Reservation and Customer models are fully unguarded ($guarded = [])
- **L76** (OptionsList/ExtrasList/FixedPricingList emit 'input' on every onUpdated, causing excessive parent notifications) also covers:
  - vue-fieldtypes-composables: Child list components emit 'input' that no parent listens to (dead emit)
- **L94** (Affiliate cookie value is unsigned and missing explicit SameSite/Secure/HttpOnly intent) also covers:
  - xc-security: Affiliate cookie set from reflected query param without normalization
- **N25** (AffiliateCpController::delete returns response(200) which sets '200' as the body, not via a clear status) also covers:
  - cp-controllers: Controllers return `response(200)` which sets the body to the string "200" rather than an empty/204 response

## Appendix B — Refuted / uncertain (do not action)

Findings a reviewer raised but the verifier could not confirm against the code. Recorded so they are not re-investigated.

- **[REFUTED]** ClearAvailabilityFieldCache forgets disabled-IDs cache but not on entry save — `src/Listeners/ClearAvailabilityFieldCache.php:11-17` _(availability-core)_
  - src/Models/Entry.php:84 `Cache::forget('resrv_disabled_entry_ids');` at the end of syncToDatabase(), which is the EntrySaved handler (AddResrvEntryToDatabase::handle -> `app(Entry::class)->syncToDatabase($event->entry)`). src/Listeners/EntryDeleted.php:30 `Cache::forget('resrv_disabled_entry_ids');`. getDisabledIds (Entry.php:117-124) caches under that key for 300s.
- **[REFUTED]** Rate ordering is grouped by (collection, base_rate_id) on write but flat by 'order' on read — `src/Models/Rate.php:162-163` _(rates)_
  - RatesList.vue:240-248 `topLevel = rates.filter(r => !r.base_rate_id).sort(order)` and `children: rates.filter(r => String(r.base_rate_id) === String(parent.id)).sort(order)`; :24 `:group="{ name: 'rate-parents', pull: false, put: false }"`; :77 `:group="{ name: 'rate-children-' + parent.id, ... }"`; :278 `newOrder = event.moved.newIndex + 1`. Rate.php:162-163 scopes changeOrder() to `where('collection')->where('base_rate_id')`.
- **[REFUTED]** getSpecificItemCollection dereferences a possibly-null entry — `src/Models/Availability.php:338-344` _(rates)_
  - Entry.php:47-50 `public static function whereItemId(string $id): ?static { return static::query()->itemId($id)->firstOrFail(); }` — firstOrFail() throws, never returns null. Availability.php:338 `$resrvEntry = Entry::whereItemId($statamic_id);` then :344 `if ($resrvEntry->isDisabled())`.
- **[REFUTED]** checkout() with extraDays always selects the offset-0 period regardless of user choice — `src/Livewire/AvailabilityResults.php:153-177` _(livewire-availability)_
  - Line 156: `$this->availability = collect($this->availability->get(0));` only collapses; checkout uses $this->data (search dates). Blade availability-results.blade.php renders one availability blob (line 45 pricing partial) + one `wire:click="checkout()"` (line 52), no per-period booking UI. Test AvailabilityResultsTest.php:991-1021 sets extraDays=1/extraDaysOffset=1 and asserts assertDatabaseHas with `'date_start' => $this->date` and `'price' => data_get($availability[0],'data.price')` — the offset-0 period, confirming intended behavior.
- **[REFUTED]** confirmReservationHasNotExpired throws without freeing availability or cancelling the intent — `src/Livewire/Checkout.php:514-520` _(livewire-checkout)_
  - Checkout.php:116-120 reservation() is #[Computed] → getReservation(). HandlesReservationQueries.php:57-64 calls $reservation->expire() and throws when expireAt <= now. expire() (Reservation.php:568-612) frees stock and cancels the intent. confirmReservationHasNotExpired (514-520) is reached only after $this->reservation resolves through getReservation.
- **[REFUTED]** customer_data v-for can iterate a numerically-indexed array, mislabeling fields — `resources/js/pages/Reservations/Show.vue:117, 124-130` _(vue-pages)_
  - getCustomerDataAttribute (Reservation.php:120-123): `$data = $customer->data; $data->put('email', $customer->email); return $data;` - associative handles. Controller (lines 135-137): `'customer_data' => $reservation->customer_data->reject(fn ($value) => is_array($value) || $value === null)->all(),` - reject() preserves keys, no reindexing.
- **[REFUTED]** DynamicPricingPanel Extras 'Select all/Clear' actions are placed in a non-existent slot of Field, not Combobox — `resources/js/components/DynamicPricingPanel.vue:73-89` _(vue-components-data)_
  - vendor Field.vue:99 `<div v-if="label || (instructions && !instructionsBelow) || $slots.label || $slots.actions">` and :111 `<slot name="actions" />`. MassAvailabilityModal.vue:4-7 uses the identical `<Field><template #actions>` pattern successfully.
- **[UNCERTAIN]** Availability/Cutoff switches do not react to external value changes — `resources/js/fieldtypes/Availability.vue:59-60` _(vue-fieldtypes-composables)_
  - Availability.vue:59-60 `const enabled = ref(props.value || 'disabled'); const reservationsEnabled = ref(enabled.value !== 'disabled');` with no watch on props.value (grep shows watchers only on rateId, line 172). Cutoff.vue:99-104 loads via loadExistingSettings() only in onMounted; the only props watcher is the deep watch on local `settings` (line 106), not props.value. Whether Statamic remounts these on revision/localization changes is not demonstrable from the reviewed code.
